
#Scripted effects for Mod

random_list_option = {
   remove_all_random_list_flags = yes
   add_country_modifier = {
      name = option_$option$
      duration = 2
      hidden = yes
   }
}
remove_all_random_list_flags = {
   remove_country_modifier = option_1
   remove_country_modifier = option_2
   remove_country_modifier = option_3
   remove_country_modifier = option_4
   remove_country_modifier = option_5
   remove_country_modifier = option_6
   remove_country_modifier = option_7
   remove_country_modifier = option_8
   remove_country_modifier = option_9
   remove_country_modifier = option_10
   remove_country_modifier = option_11
   remove_country_modifier = option_12
   remove_country_modifier = option_13
   remove_country_modifier = option_14
   remove_country_modifier = option_15
   remove_country_modifier = option_16
   remove_country_modifier = option_17
   remove_country_modifier = option_18
   remove_country_modifier = option_19
   remove_country_modifier = option_20
}

randomise_world_development_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = { 
         ai = no 
         NOT = { has_country_flag = world_dev_random }
      }
      set_country_flag = world_dev_random
      set_desired_regional_development = yes
      set_calculated_regional_development = yes
   }
}
set_regional_development = {
   set_variable = {
      which = $region$_development
      value = $development$
   }
}

regional_development_effect = {
   roll_dice_effect = { region = $region$ }
   calc_development_from_diceroll = { region = $region$ }
   add_regional_development = { region = $region$ }
   add_random_trade_centres = { region = $region$ }
}

roll_dice_effect = {
   # roll a dice from 0-10
   random_list = {
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = $region$_diceroll
            value = 0
         }
      }
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = $region$_diceroll
            value = 1
         }
      }
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = $region$_diceroll
            value = 2
         }
      }
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = $region$_diceroll
            value = 3
         }
      }
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = $region$_diceroll
            value = 4
         }
      }
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = $region$_diceroll
            value = 5
         }
      }
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = $region$_diceroll
            value = 6
         }
      }
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = $region$_diceroll
            value = 7
         }
      }
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = $region$_diceroll
            value = 8
         }
      }
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = $region$_diceroll
            value = 9
         }
      }
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = $region$_diceroll
            value = 10
         }
      }
   }
}

calc_development_from_diceroll = {
   set_variable = {
      which = $region$_development_bonus_modifier
      value = 0.05
   }
   subtract_variable = {
      which = $region$_diceroll
      value = 5
   }
   multiply_variable = {
      which = $region$_development_bonus_modifier
      which = $region$_diceroll
   }
   change_variable = {
      which = $region$_development_bonus_modifier
      value = 1
   }
   multiply_variable = {
      which = $region$_development
      which = $region$_development_bonus_modifier
   }
}
add_regional_development = {
   while = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = {
            which = $region$_development
            value = 1
         }
      }
      random_list = {
         37 = {
            trigger = {
               random_list_trigger = { option = 1 }
            }
            random_list_option = {     option = 1 }
            # add_base_tax = 1
            change_regional_dev_province = {
               region = $region$
               type = tax
               amount = 1
            }
         }
         24 = {
            trigger = {
               random_list_trigger = { option = 2 }
            }
            random_list_option = {     option = 2 }
            # add_base_production = 1
            change_regional_dev_province = {
               region = $region$
               type = production
               amount = 1
            }
         }
         12 = {
            trigger = {
               random_list_trigger = { option = 3 }
            }
            random_list_option = {     option = 3 }
            # add_base_manpower = 1
            change_regional_dev_province = {
               region = $region$
               type = manpower
               amount = 1
            }
         }
         12 = {
            trigger = {
               random_list_trigger = { option = 4 }
            }
            random_list_option = {     option = 4 }
            #nothing
         }
         5 = {
            trigger = {
               random_list_trigger = { option = 5 }
            }
            random_list_option = {     option = 5 }
            # add_base_tax = 2
            change_regional_dev_province = {
               region = $region$
               type = tax
               amount = 2
            }
         }
         4 = {
            trigger = {
               random_list_trigger = { option = 6 }
            }
            random_list_option = {     option = 6 }
            # add_base_production = 2
            change_regional_dev_province = {
               region = $region$
               type = production
               amount = 2
            }
         }
         2 = {
            trigger = {
               random_list_trigger = { option = 7 }
            }
            random_list_option = {     option = 7 }
            # add_base_manpower = 2
            change_regional_dev_province = {
               region = $region$
               type = manpower
               amount = 2
            }
         }
      }
   }
}
change_regional_dev_province = {
   random_province = {
      limit = { region = $region$ }
      add_development_effect = {
         type = $type$
         amount = $amount$
      }
   }
   subtract_variable = {
      which = $region$_development
      value = $amount$
   }
}

add_development_effect = {
   set_variable = {
      which = ForLoopCounter
      value = $amount$
   }
   if = {
      limit = { is_empty = no }
      while = {
         limit = {
            check_variable = {
               which = ForLoopCounter
               value = 1
            }
         }
         subtract_variable = {
            which = ForLoopCounter
            value = 1
         }
         add_base_$type$ = 1
         add_next_institution_embracement = 3.6
         owner = { change_estate_land_share = { estate = all share = -0.1 } }
         on_$type$_development_effect = yes
      }
   }
   else = {
      while = {
         limit = {
            check_variable = {
               which = ForLoopCounter
               value = 1
            }
         }
         subtract_variable = {
            which = ForLoopCounter
            value = 1
         }
         add_base_$type$ = 1
      }
   }
}

# Triggered from add_development_effect and on_$type$_development in on_actions.txt
on_tax_development_effect = {
   clear_institution_target = yes
}
on_production_development_effect = {
   clear_institution_target = yes
}
on_manpower_development_effect = {
   clear_institution_target = yes
}

# randomises where trade centres are on startup.
add_random_trade_centres = {
   $region$ = {
      random_list = {
         90 = { add_center_of_trade_level = 0 } #nothing
         10 = { 
            modifier = {
               factor = 0.6
               any_neighbor_province = {
                  province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
               }
            } 
            center_of_trade = 1 
         }
         2 = {
            modifier = {
               factor = 2
               has_port = yes
            }
            center_of_trade = 2 
         }
      }
      random_list = {
         90 = { add_center_of_trade_level = 0 } #nothing
         2.5 = {
            trigger = { has_port = yes }
            modifier = {
               factor = 3
               NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
               NOT = {
                  any_neighbor_province = {
                     province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
                  }
               }
            }
            add_permanent_province_modifier = {
               name = "important_estuary_modifier"
               duration = -1
            }
         }
         1.75 = {
            modifier = {
               factor = 0.5
               has_port = yes
            }
            modifier = {
               factor = 3
               NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
               NOT = {
                  any_neighbor_province = {
                     province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
                  }
               }
            }
            add_permanent_province_modifier = {
               name = "important_trade_route_modifier"
               duration = -1
            }
         }
      }
   }
}





randomise_country_effects = {
   if = {
      limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = randomised_country_fl } }
      set_country_flag = randomised_country_fl

      randomise_estates_effect = yes #switchup privileges & crownland
      randomise_reforms_effect = yes #switchup government reforms
      randomise_ideas_effect = yes #switchup idea groups
      # every country starts with a fort randomly dumped somewhere
      random_owned_province = {
         add_building_construction = { building = fort_15th speed = 0 cost = 0 }
      }
      # random chance of getting feudalism in your capital at game start
      random = {
         chance = 35
         capital_scope = {
            add_institution_embracement = {
               which = feudalism
               value = 100
            }
         }
      }
   }
}
randomise_estates_effect = {
   randomise_crownland_effect = yes
   randomise_estate_privileges = yes
}
randomise_crownland_effect = {
   change_estate_land_share = { # set crownland to 0
      estate = all
      share = 25
   }
   set_variable = {
      which = country_crownland
      value = 25 # base value
   }
   set_variable = {
      which = country_crownland_modifier
      value = 0.1
   }
   crownland_random_list_effect = yes
   subtract_variable = {
      which = crownland_diceroll
      value = 6
   }
   multiply_variable = {
      which = country_crownland_modifier
      which = crownland_diceroll
   }
   change_variable = {
      which = country_crownland_modifier
      value = 1
   }
   # now we have the new desired value of crownland
   multiply_variable = {
      which = country_crownland
      which = country_crownland_modifier
   }
   while = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = {
            which = country_crownland
            value = 2.5
         }
      }
      subtract_variable = {
         which = country_crownland
         value = 2.5
      }
      change_estate_land_share = {
         estate = all
         share = -2.5
      }
   }
}

randomise_estate_privileges = {
   # Randomises the estate privileges you have access to throughout a campaign
   random_list = {
      1 = { set_country_flag = estate_privileges_1 }
      1 = { set_country_flag = estate_privileges_2 }
      1 = { set_country_flag = estate_privileges_3 }
   }
}
randomise_reforms_effect = {
   # Randomises the government reforms you have access to throughout a campaign
   random_list = {
      1 = { set_country_flag = government_reforms_1 }
      1 = { set_country_flag = government_reforms_2 }
      1 = { set_country_flag = government_reforms_3 }
   }
}
randomise_ideas_effect = {
   # Randomises the idea groups you have access to throughout a campaign
   random_list = {
      1 = { set_country_flag = idea_group_1 }
      1 = { set_country_flag = idea_group_2 }
      1 = { set_country_flag = idea_group_3 }
   }
}

# This is useful if you want to add piety depending on which side you are leaning towards.
# make sure $amount$ is not negative!
add_piety_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = { piety = 0.01 }
      add_piety = $amount$
   }
   else = { add_piety = -$amount$ }
}
#opposite effect
remove_piety_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = { piety = 0.01 }
      add_piety = -$amount$
   }
   else = { add_piety = $amount$ }
}

# I've set this up because using too many country flags for events bloats the country shield view when in debug_mode. Rather keep that clean as possible.
set_event_flag = {
   add_country_modifier = {
      name = $event$
      duration = -1
      hidden = yes
   }
}

# scopes to a random estate in the country. Can accept type <military|administrative|economic> to break down estates.
# can be used to apply loyalty, land share and influence.
# will slowly incorporate other estate scripted effects into this one
random_estate = {
   custom_tooltip = a_random_estate_[[type]$type$]
   [[add_loyalty]custom_tooltip = loc_estate_L$add_loyalty$]
   [[add_influence]custom_tooltip = loc_estate_I$add_influence$]
   [[add_land_share]custom_tooltip = loc_estate_S$add_land_share$]
   hidden_effect = {
      [[type] set_country_flag = estate_$type$ ]
      random_list = {
         #military estates
         1 = {
            trigger = { has_estate = estate_nobles [[type] has_country_flag = estate_military_estate ] }
            [[add_loyalty]    add_estate_loyalty = {           estate = estate_nobles loyalty = $add_loyalty$ } ]
            [[add_land_share] change_estate_land_share = {     estate = estate_nobles share = $add_land_share$ } ]
            [[add_influence]  add_estate_influence_modifier={  estate = estate_nobles influence=$add_influence$ desc=$desc$ duration=$duration$}]
         }
         1 = {
            trigger = { has_estate = estate_maratha [[type] has_country_flag = estate_military_estate ] }
            [[add_loyalty]    add_estate_loyalty = {           estate = estate_maratha loyalty = $add_loyalty$ } ]
            [[add_land_share] change_estate_land_share = {     estate = estate_maratha share = $add_land_share$ } ]
            [[add_influence]  add_estate_influence_modifier={  estate = estate_maratha influence=$add_influence$ desc=$desc$ duration=$duration$}]
         }
         1 = {
            trigger = { has_estate = estate_nomadic_tribes [[type] has_country_flag = estate_military_estate ] }
            [[add_loyalty]    add_estate_loyalty = {           estate = estate_nomadic_tribes loyalty = $add_loyalty$ } ]
            [[add_land_share] change_estate_land_share = {     estate = estate_nomadic_tribes share = $add_land_share$ } ]
            [[add_influence]  add_estate_influence_modifier={  estate = estate_nomadic_tribes influence=$add_influence$ desc=$desc$ duration=$duration$}]
         }
         1 = {
            trigger = { has_estate = estate_rajput [[type] has_country_flag = estate_military_estate ] }
            [[add_loyalty]    add_estate_loyalty = {           estate = estate_rajput loyalty = $add_loyalty$ } ]
            [[add_land_share] change_estate_land_share = {     estate = estate_rajput share = $add_land_share$ } ]
            [[add_influence]  add_estate_influence_modifier={  estate = estate_rajput influence=$add_influence$ desc=$desc$ duration=$duration$}]
         }
         1 = {
            trigger = { has_estate = estate_cossacks [[type] has_country_flag = estate_military_estate ] }
            [[add_loyalty]    add_estate_loyalty = {           estate = estate_cossacks loyalty = $add_loyalty$ } ]
            [[add_land_share] change_estate_land_share = {     estate = estate_cossacks share = $add_land_share$ } ]
            [[add_influence]  add_estate_influence_modifier={  estate = estate_cossacks influence=$add_influence$ desc=$desc$ duration=$duration$}]
         }
         #administrative estates
         1 = {
            trigger = { has_estate = estate_brahmins [[type] has_country_flag = estate_administrative_estate ] }
            [[add_loyalty]    add_estate_loyalty = {           estate = estate_brahmins loyalty = $add_loyalty$ } ]
            [[add_land_share] change_estate_land_share = {     estate = estate_brahmins share = $add_land_share$ } ]
            [[add_influence]  add_estate_influence_modifier={  estate = estate_brahmins influence=$add_influence$ desc=$desc$ duration=$duration$}]
         }
         1 = {
            trigger = { has_estate = estate_church [[type] has_country_flag = estate_administrative_estate ] }
            [[add_loyalty]    add_estate_loyalty = {           estate = estate_church loyalty = $add_loyalty$ } ]
            [[add_land_share] change_estate_land_share = {     estate = estate_church share = $add_land_share$ } ]
            [[add_influence]  add_estate_influence_modifier={  estate = estate_church influence=$add_influence$ desc=$desc$ duration=$duration$}]
         }
         1 = {
            trigger = { has_estate = estate_eunuchs [[type] has_country_flag = estate_administrative_estate ] }
            [[add_loyalty]    add_estate_loyalty = {           estate = estate_eunuchs loyalty = $add_loyalty$ } ]
            [[add_land_share] change_estate_land_share = {     estate = estate_eunuchs share = $add_land_share$ } ]
            [[add_influence]  add_estate_influence_modifier={  estate = estate_eunuchs influence=$add_influence$ desc=$desc$ duration=$duration$}]
         }
         1 = {
            trigger = { has_estate = estate_dhimmi [[type] has_country_flag = estate_administrative_estate ] }
            [[add_loyalty]    add_estate_loyalty = {           estate = estate_dhimmi loyalty = $add_loyalty$ } ]
            [[add_land_share] change_estate_land_share = {     estate = estate_dhimmi share = $add_land_share$ } ]
            [[add_influence]  add_estate_influence_modifier={  estate = estate_dhimmi influence=$add_influence$ desc=$desc$ duration=$duration$}]
         }
         #economic estates
         1 = {
            trigger = { has_estate = estate_burghers [[type] has_country_flag = estate_economic_estate ] }
            [[add_loyalty]    add_estate_loyalty = {           estate = estate_burghers loyalty = $add_loyalty$ } ]
            [[add_land_share] change_estate_land_share = {     estate = estate_burghers share = $add_land_share$ } ]
            [[add_influence]  add_estate_influence_modifier={  estate = estate_burghers influence=$add_influence$ desc=$desc$ duration=$duration$}]
         }
         1 = {
            trigger = { has_estate = estate_jains [[type] has_country_flag = estate_economic_estate ] }
            [[add_loyalty]    add_estate_loyalty = {           estate = estate_jains loyalty = $add_loyalty$ } ]
            [[add_land_share] change_estate_land_share = {     estate = estate_jains share = $add_land_share$ } ]
            [[add_influence]  add_estate_influence_modifier={  estate = estate_jains influence=$add_influence$ desc=$desc$ duration=$duration$}]
         }
         1 = {
            trigger = { has_estate = estate_vaisyas [[type] has_country_flag = estate_economic_estate ] }
            [[add_loyalty]    add_estate_loyalty = {           estate = estate_vaisyas loyalty = $add_loyalty$ } ]
            [[add_land_share] change_estate_land_share = {     estate = estate_vaisyas share = $add_land_share$ } ]
            [[add_influence]  add_estate_influence_modifier={  estate = estate_vaisyas influence=$add_influence$ desc=$desc$ duration=$duration$}]
         }
      }
      [[type] clr_country_flag = estate_$type$ ]
   }
}

#Removes Revolution from all Primary Culture provinces 
french_mechanic_remove_revolution_from_province_effect = {
	hidden_effect = { set_revolution_in_province = no }
	add_province_modifier = {
		name = no_revolution_here_dummy
		duration = 7300
		hidden = yes
	}
}

}

upgrade_cultural_center_effect = { #upgrades cultural centers
   set_province_flag = tier_1_cultural_center
   subtract_variable = { which = culture_var value = $value$ }
   set_great_project_tier_$level$ = { type = el_escorial }
   set_great_project_tier_$level$ = { type = ait_benhaddou }
   set_great_project_tier_$level$ = { type = tower_of_london }
   set_great_project_tier_$level$ = { type = versailles }
   set_great_project_tier_$level$ = { type = stonehenge }
   set_great_project_tier_$level$ = { type = stpeters_cathedral }
   set_great_project_tier_$level$ = { type = porcelain_tower_nanjing }
   set_great_project_tier_$level$ = { type = gyeongbok_palace }

   set_great_project_tier_$level$ = { type = erdene_zuu }
   set_great_project_tier_$level$ = { type = mount_fuji }
}

change_num_of_revoked_privileges = {
   if = {
      limit = {
         NOT = {
            check_variable = {
               which = estate_revoke_var
               value = 0
            }
         }
      }
      set_variable = {
         which = estate_revoke_var
         value = $amount$
      }
   }
   else = {
      change_variable = {
         which = estate_revoke_var
         value = $amount$
      }
   }
}
on_privilege_revoke_cac_effect = {
   hidden_effect = {
      country_event = {
         id = cac.1 #Starts CAC, if not active
      }
   }
   if = {
      limit = { has_country_flag = in_court_and_country }
      hidden_effect = {
         random_owned_province = {
            limit = { 
               is_island = no
               if = {
                  limit = { owner = { ai = yes } }
                  same_continent = capital
               }
               NOT = { has_province_modifier = CAC_no_revolt_here_dummy }
            }
            start_revolt = { size = 3 }
            add_province_modifier = {
               name = CAC_no_revolt_here_dummy
               duration = 3650
               hidden = yes
            }
         }
      }
   }
}
#Revoke estate privilege variable
absolutism_revoke_effect = {
   change_num_of_revoked_privileges = {
      amount = 1
   }
   on_privilege_revoke_cac_effect = yes
}
#Clears privilege revoke variable
clear_absolutism_revoke_effect = {
   set_variable = {
      which = estate_revoke_var
      value = 0
   }
}
slavery_randomize_effect = { #Provinces that produce slaves in the ivory coast will change to a random trade good
   1466 = {
      every_trade_node_member_province = {
         limit = { trade_goods = slaves }
         random_list = {
            20 = { change_trade_goods = ivory }
            20 = { change_trade_goods = grain }
            20 = { change_trade_goods = sugar }
            20 = { change_trade_goods = tropical_wood }
            20 = { change_trade_goods = fish }        
         }
         set_province_flag = no_more_slaves_here
      }
   }
}
alm_set_estate_privileges_effect = { #Used for the on_province_owner_change on action
	if = {
	   limit = {
	      owner = { has_country_flag = estate_burghers_alm_black_gold }
	      trade_goods = coffee
	   }
	   add_province_modifier = {
	      name = estate_burghers_alm_black_gold
	      duration = -1
	   }
	}
   if = {
      limit = {
         owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_faiths_bastion }
         religion = orthodox
         NOT = { has_province_modifier = faiths_bastion_mod }
      }
      add_province_modifier = {
         name = faiths_bastion_mod
         duration = -1
      }
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_eunuchs_harmonize_folk_religions }
         religion = shen
         NOT = { has_province_modifier = eunuchs_harmonize_folk_religions_mod }
      }
      add_province_modifier = {
         name = eunuchs_harmonize_folk_religions_mod
         duration = -1
      }
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_trade_leniency }
         province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
         NOT = { has_province_modifier = burghers_trade_leniency_mod }
      }
      add_province_modifier = {
         name = burghers_trade_leniency_mod
         duration = -1
      }
   }
}
alm_religion_converted_privileges_effect = { #Used for the on_province_religion_converted on action
   if = {
      limit = {
         owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_faiths_bastion }
         religion = orthodox
         NOT = { has_province_modifier = faiths_bastion_mod }
      }
      add_province_modifier = {
         name = faiths_bastion_mod
         duration = -1
      }
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         has_province_modifier = faiths_bastion_mod
         NOT = { religion = orthodox }
      }
      remove_province_modifier = faiths_bastion_mod
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_eunuchs_harmonize_folk_religions }
         religion = shen
         NOT = { has_province_modifier = eunuchs_harmonize_folk_religions_mod }
      }
      add_province_modifier = {
         name = eunuchs_harmonize_folk_religions_mod
         duration = -1
      }
   }
   if = {
      limit = { 
         has_province_modifier = eunuchs_harmonize_folk_religions_mod
         NOT = { religion = shen }
      }
      remove_province_modifier = eunuchs_harmonize_folk_religions_mod
   }
}     
alm_coffee_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = {
         owner = { has_country_flag = estate_burghers_alm_black_gold }
         trade_goods = coffee
         NOT = { has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_alm_black_gold }
      }
      add_province_modifier = {
         name = estate_burghers_alm_black_gold 
         duration = -1
      }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = {
         NOT = { trade_goods = coffee }
         has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_alm_black_gold
      }
      remove_province_modifier = estate_burghers_alm_black_gold
   }
}

clear_CAC_triggers = { #Clears all related Court and Country triggers
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_1
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_2
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_3
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_4
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_5
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_6
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_7
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_8
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_9
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_10
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_11
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_12
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_13
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_14
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_15
   clr_country_flag = CAC_event_16
   clr_country_flag = CAC_broke_to_rebels
   clr_country_flag = CAC_republic_chose_monarchy
   clr_country_flag = CAC_republic_chose_republic
   clr_country_flag = authority_questioned
   clr_country_flag = authority_imposed
   if = { 
      limit = {
         OR = {
            check_variable = {
               which = republic_support_var
               value = 1
            }
            check_variable = {
               which = monarchy_support_var
               value = 1
            }
         }
      }
      set_variable = {
         which = republic_support_var
         value = 0
      }
      set_variable = {
         which = monarchy_support_var
         value = 0
      }
   }
}
add_great_wall_of_china_modifier = {
   if = {
      limit = {
         has_province_flag = the_great_wall_of_china
         culture_group = east_asian
         has_fort_building_trigger = yes
         owner = { 
            culture_group = east_asian
            owns_core_province = 698
         }
      }
      if = {
         limit = {
            698 = {
               has_great_project = {
                  tier = 0
                  type = the_great_wall_of_china
               }
            }
         }
         remove_great_wall_of_china_modifier = yes
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = {
            698 = {
               has_great_project = {
                  tier = 1
                  type = the_great_wall_of_china
               }
            }
         }
         remove_great_wall_of_china_modifier = yes
         add_province_modifier = {
            name = great_wall_of_china_t1
            duration = -1
         }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = {
            698 = {
               has_great_project = {
                  tier = 2
                  type = the_great_wall_of_china
               }
            }
         }
         remove_great_wall_of_china_modifier = yes
         add_province_modifier = {
            name = great_wall_of_china_t2
            duration = -1
         }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = {
            698 = {
               has_great_project = {
                  tier = 3
                  type = the_great_wall_of_china
               }
            }
         }
         remove_great_wall_of_china_modifier = yes
         add_province_modifier = {
            name = great_wall_of_china_t3
            duration = -1
         }
      }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = {
         has_province_flag = the_great_wall_of_china
      }
      remove_great_wall_of_china_modifier = yes
   }
}
remove_great_wall_of_china_modifier = {
   if = {
      limit = {
         has_province_flag = the_great_wall_of_china
      }
      remove_province_modifier = great_wall_of_china_t1
      remove_province_modifier = great_wall_of_china_t2
      remove_province_modifier = great_wall_of_china_t3
   }
}
on_action_great_wall_of_china = {
   if = {
		limit = {
			province_id = 698
			culture_group = east_asian
			owner = { culture_group = east_asian }
		}
      china_superregion = {
         add_great_wall_of_china_modifier = yes
      }
      manchuria_region = {
         add_great_wall_of_china_modifier = yes
      }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			province_id = 698
		}
		china_superregion = {
			remove_great_wall_of_china_modifier = yes
		}
		manchuria_region = {
			remove_great_wall_of_china_modifier = yes
		}
	}
   else = {
      add_great_wall_of_china_modifier = yes
   }
}

independent_tags_drop_mandate_effect = {
   china_superregion = {
      limit = {
         owner = {
            is_emperor_of_china = no
            NOT = { has_reform = chinese_warlord_reform }
         }
      }
      set_province_flag = china_held_by_independent
   }
   set_variable = {
      which = china_held_by_independent_var
      value = 0
   }
   add_country_modifier = {
      name = independent_mandate_0
      hidden = yes
      duration = -1
   }
   while = {
      limit = {
         china_superregion = {
            has_province_flag = china_held_by_independent
         }
      }
      random_province = {
         limit = { has_province_flag = china_held_by_independent }
         clr_province_flag = china_held_by_independent
      }
      change_variable = {
         which = china_held_by_independent_var
         value = 1
      }
   }
   while = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = {
            which = china_held_by_independent_var
            value = 1
         }
      }
      subtract_variable = {
         which = china_held_by_independent_var
         value = 2
      }
      trigger_switch = {
         on_trigger = has_country_modifier
         independent_mandate_0 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_0 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_2 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }
         independent_mandate_2 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_2 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_4 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }
         independent_mandate_4 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_4 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_6 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }
         independent_mandate_6 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_6 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_8 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }
         independent_mandate_8 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_8 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_10 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }
         independent_mandate_10 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_10 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_12 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }
         independent_mandate_12 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_12 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_14 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }
         independent_mandate_14 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_14 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_16 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }
         independent_mandate_16 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_16 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_18 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }
         independent_mandate_18 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_18 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_20 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }
         independent_mandate_20 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_20 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_22 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }
         independent_mandate_22 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_22 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_24 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }
         independent_mandate_24 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_24 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_26 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }
         independent_mandate_26 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_26 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_28 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }
         independent_mandate_28 = { remove_country_modifier = independent_mandate_28 add_country_modifier = { name = independent_mandate_30 hidden = yes duration = -1 } }

increase_mandate_from_won_war_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = {
         FROM = {
            OR = {
               has_reform = chinese_warlord_reform
               any_core_province = {
                  superregion = china_superregion
                  NOT = { owned_by = FROM }
               }
            }
         }
      }
      add_mandate = 5
   }
}
dismantle_empire_of_china_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = {
         OR = {
            has_reform = chinese_warlord_reform
            AND = {
               capital_scope = { superregion = china_superregion }
               culture_group = east_asian
            }
         }
         is_subject = no
      }
      set_emperor_of_china = ROOT
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						tag = ROOT
                  tag = FROM
					}
				}
            capital_scope = { superregion = china_superregion }
			}
         add_government_reform = chinese_warlord_reform
         add_meritocracy = 100
		}
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = {
         any_known_country = {
            NOT = { tag = FROM }
            OR = {
               has_reform = chinese_warlord_reform
               AND = {
                  capital_scope = { superregion = china_superregion }
                  culture_group = east_asian
               }
            }
         }
      }
      random_country = {
         limit = {
            OR = {
               has_reform = chinese_warlord_reform
               AND = {
                  capital_scope = { superregion = china_superregion }
                  culture_group = east_asian
               }
            }
            NOT = { tag = FROM }
            NOT = {
               any_known_country = {
                  NOT = { tag = PREV }
                  NOT = { tag = FROM }
                  OR = {
                     has_reform = chinese_warlord_reform
                     AND = {
                        capital_scope = { superregion = china_superregion }
                        culture_group = east_asian
                     }
                  }
                  total_development = PREV
               }
            }
         }
         set_emperor_of_china = THIS
		   every_known_country = {
			   limit = {
				   NOT = { 
					   OR = {
						   tag = PREV
                     tag = FROM
					   }
				   }
               capital_scope = { superregion = china_superregion }
			   }
            add_government_reform = chinese_warlord_reform
            add_meritocracy = 100
			}
      }
   }
   else = {
      dismantle_empire_of_china = yes
		set_global_flag = empire_of_china_dismantled
   }
}
eoc_miao_rebellions_effect = {
   if = {
		limit = {
			culture = miao
			NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = eoc_defeated_miao } }
         NOT = { exists = CMI }
		}
      set_country_flag = spawn_miao_flag
		owner = { country_event = { id = eoc_events.2 } } #Miao declares independence
	}
   if = {
      limit = {
			culture = yi
			NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = eoc_defeated_yi } }
         NOT = { exists = CYI }
		}
      set_country_flag = spawn_yi_flag
		owner = { country_event = { id = eoc_events.2 } } #Yi declares independence
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         culture = bai
         NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = eoc_defeated_bai } }
         NOT = { exists = CDL }
      }
      set_country_flag = spawn_dali_flag
      owner = { country_event = { id = eoc_events.2 } } #Dali declares independence
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         culture = zhuang
         NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = eoc_defeated_zhuang } }
         NOT = { exists = CGS }
      }
      set_country_flag = spawn_changseng_flag
      owner = { country_event = { id = eoc_events.2 } } #Changseng declares independence
   }
}
on_action_miao_revolts_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = {
         has_province_flag = local_miao_revolts
         owner = { has_country_flag = eoc_not_exterminating_miao }
      }
      if = {
         limit = {
            culture_group = tibetan_group
            NOT = { province_is_or_accepts_culture = yes }
            NOT = { has_province_modifier = eoc_local_miao_revolts }
         }
         add_province_modifier = {
            name = eoc_local_miao_revolts
            duration = -1
            desc = prov_miao_revolts_desc
         }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = {
            has_province_modifier = eoc_local_miao_revolts
            province_is_or_accepts_culture = yes
         }
         remove_province_modifier = eoc_local_miao_revolts
      }
   }
}
eoc_defeated_revolt_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = { FROM = { tag = CMI } }
      set_country_flag = eoc_defeated_miao
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = { FROM = { tag = CYI } }
      set_country_flag = eoc_defeated_yi
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = { FROM = { tag = CDL } }
      set_country_flag = eoc_defeated_bai
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = { FROM = { tag = CGS } }
      set_country_flag = eoc_defeated_zhuang
   }
}
eoc_play_as_warlord_effect = {
   clr_country_flag = eoc_exterminating_miao
   set_country_flag = eoc_not_exterminating_miao
   hidden_effect = {
      china_superregion = {
         limit = {
            culture_group = tibetan_group
            owned_by = ROOT
         }
         set_province_flag = local_miao_revolts
         add_province_modifier = {
            name = eoc_local_miao_revolts
            duration = -1
            desc = prov_miao_revolts_desc
         } 
      }
      declare_war_with_cb = {
         casus_belli = cb_crush_rebel_warlord
         who = $who$
      }
      switch_tag = $who$
   }
}

   clr_country_flag = eoc_exterminating_miao
	clr_country_flag = eoc_not_exterminating_miao
	clr_country_flag = eoc_defeated_miao
	clr_country_flag = eoc_defeated_bai
	clr_country_flag = eoc_defeated_yi
	clr_country_flag = eoc_defeated_zhuang
	CMI = { clr_country_flag = miao_fighting_emperor }
	CYI = { clr_country_flag = miao_fighting_emperor }
	CDL = { clr_country_flag = miao_fighting_emperor }
	CGS = { clr_country_flag = miao_fighting_emperor }
   china_superregion = {
      limit = {
         OR = {
            has_province_modifier = eoc_local_miao_revolts
            has_province_flag = local_miao_revolts
         }
      }
      remove_province_modifier = eoc_local_miao_revolts
      clr_province_flag = local_miao_revolts
   }
	remove_country_modifier = eoc_miao_revolts_modifier
	remove_country_modifier = eoc_fighting_miao_rebels
	every_owned_province = {
		limit = { has_province_modifier = eoc_converting_miao_modifier }
		remove_province_modifier = eoc_converting_miao_modifier
	}
}

unrest_in_chinese_provinces_effect = {
   if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_reform = khanganate_reform }
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = unrest_in_chinese_provinces }
			culture_group = east_asian
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = unrest_in_chinese_provinces
			hidden = yes
			duration = -1
		}
	}
   if = {
      limit = {
         has_province_modifier = unrest_in_chinese_provinces
         OR = {
            owner = { NOT = { has_reform = khanganate_reform } }
            NOT = { culture_group = east_asian }
         }
      }
      remove_province_modifier = unrest_in_chinese_provinces
   }
}

sinify_culture_to = {
   custom_tooltip = change_to_chinese_group_tooltip
   hidden_effect = {
      every_province = {
         limit = { culture = ROOT }
         change_culture = $culture$
      }
      every_country = {
         limit = { 
            primary_culture = ROOT
            NOT = { tag = ROOT }
         }
         change_primary_culture = $culture$
         set_ruler_culture = $culture$
         if = {
            limit = { has_heir = yes }
            set_heir_culture = $culture$
         }
         if = {
            limit = { has_consort = yes }
            set_consort_culture = $culture$
         }
      }
      change_primary_culture = $culture$
      set_ruler_culture = $culture$
      if = {
         limit = { has_heir = yes }
         set_heir_culture = $culture$
      }
      if = {
         limit = { has_consort = yes }
         set_consort_culture = $culture$
      }
   }
}
clr_tumu_crisis_triggers = {
   clr_country_flag = tumu_crisis_victory
   clr_country_flag = tumu_crisis_failure
   clr_country_flag = captured_mng_emperor
   clr_country_flag = oir_demands_sent
   MNG = {
      if = {
         limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = mng_appointed_new_emperor } }
         set_ruler = mng_exiled_ruler
         if = {
            limit = { has_country_flag = mng_exiled_heir_flag } 
            set_heir = mng_exiled_heir
         }
         if = {
            limit = { has_ruler_flag = mng_tumu_crisis }
            clr_ruler_flag = mng_tumu_crisis
         }
      }
      clr_country_flag = mng_exiled_heir_flag
      clr_country_flag = mng_appointed_new_emperor
      clr_country_flag = mng_emperor_captured
   }
}
qng_han_banners_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = {
         owner = { 
            has_country_flag = established_han_banners
         }
         NOT = { has_province_modifier = qng_han_banners }
         NOT = { has_province_modifier = ai_qng_han_banners }
         culture_group = east_asian
      }
      if = {
         limit = { owner = { ai = yes } }
         add_province_modifier = {
            name = ai_qng_han_banners
            duration = -1
            hidden = yes
         }
      }
      else = {
         add_province_modifier = {
            name = qng_han_banners
            duration = -1
            hidden = yes
         }
      }
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         OR = {
            has_province_modifier = qng_han_banners
            has_province_modifier = ai_qng_han_banners
         }
         OR = {
            NOT = { culture_group = east_asian }
            NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = established_han_banners } }
         }
      }
      remove_province_modifier = qng_han_banners
      remove_province_modifier = ai_qng_han_banners
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         culture_group = east_asian
         owner = { has_country_flag = established_han_banners }
         NOT = { culture = manchu_new }
      }
      change_culture = manchu_new
   }
}
release_rebel_warlord = {
   every_owned_province = {
      limit = {
         $who$ = {
            primary_culture = PREV
         }
         NOT = { is_core = $who$ }
      }
      add_core = $who$
   }
   every_owned_province = {
      limit = { is_core = $who$ }
      clear_rebels = yes
   }
   if = {
      limit = { NOT = { exists = $who$ } }
      release = $who$
      $who$ = {
         change_government_to_monarchy = yes
         add_government_reform = chinese_warlord_reform
         add_meritocracy = 100
         adopt_reform_progress = ROOT
         add_yearly_manpower = 15
         add_treasury = 200
         if = {
            limit = { religion = noreligion }
            capital_scope = { PREV = { change_religion = PREV } }
         }
         if = {
            limit = { primary_culture = noculture }
            capital_scope = { PREV = { change_primary_culture = PREV } }
         }
      }
   }
   else = {
      every_owned_province = {
         limit = { is_core = $who$ }
         cede_province = $who$
      }
   }
   $who$ = { 
      capital_scope = {
         build_to_forcelimit = { 
            infantry = 0.6 
            cavalry = 0.3 
            artillery = 0.1 
         }
      }
      save_event_target_as = rebeller 
   }
   [[miao_revolts]
      $who$ = {
         set_country_flag = miao_fighting_emperor
         define_ruler = { adm = 3 dip = 5 mil = 6 age = 18 dynasty = $dynasty$ }
         add_ruler_personality = inspiring_leader_personality
         define_ruler_to_general = { fire = 4 shock = 6 manuever = 5 siege = 1 }
      }
   ]
   [[join_wars_of]
      join_all_defensive_wars_of = $join_wars_of$
   ]
}
add_ae_with = { #Current scope adds or removes AE with previous scope
   hidden_effect = {
      set_variable = {
         which = ae_to_add
         value = $amount$
      }
      if = {
         limit = {
            check_variable = {
               which = ae_to_add
               value = 1
            }
         }
         while = {
            limit = {
               check_variable = {
                  which = ae_to_add
                  value = 1
               }
            }
            subtract_variable = {
               which = ae_to_add
               value = 1
            }
            add_opinion = {
               who = $scope$
               modifier = aggressive_expansion
            }
         }
      }
      if = {
         limit = {
            NOT = {
               check_variable = {
                  which = ae_to_add
                  value = 0
               }
            }
         }
         remove_opinion = {
            who = $scope$
            modifier = aggressive_expansion
         }
      }
   }
   custom_tooltip = ae_tooltip
}
break_alliance_with = { #Breaks alliance with scope
   custom_tooltip = BREAKS_ALLIANCE_TT
   if = {
      limit = {
         alliance_with = $who$
      }
      hidden_effect = {
         if = {
            limit = {
               marriage_with = $who$
            }
            break_marriage = $who$
         }
         add_mutual_opinion_modifier_effect = {
            scope_country = $who$
            opinion_modifier = break_alliance_opinion
         }
         add_trust = {
            who = $who$
            value = -100
            mutual = yes
         }
         $who$ = {
            set_ai_attitude = {
               attitude = attitude_hostile
               who = PREV
               locked = yes
            }
         }
      }
   }
}

calculate_leaders_from_vassals = {
   clr_marcher_lords_bonus = yes
   if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = vassal_leaders value = 10 } } add_country_modifier = { name = vassal_leaders_10 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
   else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = vassal_leaders value = 9 } } add_country_modifier = { name = vassal_leaders_9 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
   else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = vassal_leaders value = 8 } } add_country_modifier = { name = vassal_leaders_8 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
   else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = vassal_leaders value = 7 } } add_country_modifier = { name = vassal_leaders_7 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
   else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = vassal_leaders value = 6 } } add_country_modifier = { name = vassal_leaders_6 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
   else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = vassal_leaders value = 5 } } add_country_modifier = { name = vassal_leaders_5 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
   else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = vassal_leaders value = 4 } } add_country_modifier = { name = vassal_leaders_4 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
   else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = vassal_leaders value = 3 } } add_country_modifier = { name = vassal_leaders_3 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
   else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = vassal_leaders value = 2 } } add_country_modifier = { name = vassal_leaders_2 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
   else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = vassal_leaders value = 1 } } add_country_modifier = { name = vassal_leaders_1 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
   set_variable = { which = vassal_leaders value = 0 }
}

set_daimyo_reform = {
   hidden_effect = {
      if = {
         limit = {
            is_subject = yes
         }
         grant_independence = yes
      }
      [[daimyo]
         trigger_switch = {
            on_trigger = government
            monarchy = { add_government_reform = daimyo_reform }
            republic = { add_government_reform = r_daimyo }
            theocracy = { add_government_reform = t_daimyo }
         }
      ]
      [[indep_daimyo]
         trigger_switch = {
            on_trigger = government
            monarchy = { add_government_reform = japanese_warlord }
            republic = { add_government_reform = r_japanese_warlord }
            theocracy = { add_government_reform = t_japanese_warlord }
         }
      ]
      if = {
         limit = {
            OR = {
               is_daimyo = yes
               is_indep_daimyo = yes
            }
            1020 = { country_or_subject_holds = PREV } #Kyoto
         }
         1020 = {
            cede_province = PREV
         }
      }
   }
}
remove_daimyo_reform = {
   hidden_effect = {
      remove_government_reform = japanese_warlord
      remove_government_reform = r_japanese_warlord
      remove_government_reform = t_japanese_warlord
      remove_government_reform = daimyo_reform
      remove_government_reform = r_daimyo
      remove_government_reform = t_daimyo
   }
}
generate_cta_effect = {
   $caller$ = {
      if = {
         limit = {
            OR = {
               is_rival = $target$
               $target$ = { is_rival = $caller$ }
            }
         }
         remove_rival = $target$
         $target$ = { remove_rival = $caller$ }
      }
      add_trust = {
         who = $target$
         value = 100
         mutual = yes
      }
      $target$ = {
         set_ai_attitude = {
            attitude = attitude_friendly
            who = $caller$
            locked = yes
         }
         add_mutual_opinion_modifier_effect = {
            scope_country = $caller$
            opinion_modifier = get_along_temp
         }
      }
      create_alliance = $target$
      country_event = {
         id = cultural_events.89 #break the alliance later
         days = 90
      }
   }
}
remove_mutual_opinion_modifier_effect = {
   remove_opinion = {
      who = $scope_country$
      modifier = $opinion_modifier$
   }
   reverse_remove_opinion = {
      who = $scope_country$
      modifier = $opinion_modifier$
   }
}

calculate_rebel_size_modifier = { #Calculates local rebel size modifier
   set_variable = {
      which = rebel_size_modifier
      value = 1
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         owner = { has_idea = indirect_rule }
      }
      change_variable = {
         which = rebel_size_modifier
         value = -0.25
      }
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         owner = { 
            has_active_policy = policy_of_calculate_delay
            NOT = { has_country_modifier = reverse_policy_of_calculate_delay }
         }
      }
      change_variable = {
         which = rebel_size_modifier
         value = -0.75
      }
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         owner = { 
            ai = yes
         }
      }
      change_variable = {
         which = rebel_size_modifier
         value = -0.5 #temporary fix to some issues
      }
   }
}
start_revolt = {
   #SYNTAX:

   #Optional: Spawn a specific rebel type, or clear existing rebels in province
   # type = <rebel_type> if unspecified, will create default province revolt
   # size = <size of the rebels to use>
   # friend = <scope> | optional, assign an associated tag to the rebels
   # religion = <religion> | optional, assign a specific religion to the rebels
   # culture = <culture> | optional, assign a specific culture to the rebels
   # leader = <name> | optional, assign a leader name to the rebels
   # leader_dynasty <dynasty> | optional, assign a dynasty to the rebels
   # win = yes | optional, decides if the rebels control the province when spawned
   # should_take_capital = yes | used for special stuff
   # separatists_target <scope> | used for special stuff
   # use_monarch_as_leader = yes | optional, the monarch becomes leader of rebels
   # use_heir_as_leader = yes | optional, the heir becomes leader of rebels
   # female = yes | optional, should the rebels be femboys

   if = {
      limit = {
         always = yes
         [[pirate] always = no ]
      }
      custom_tooltip = create_revolt_effect_tt
   }
   [[pirate]
      custom_tooltip = create_pirate_effect_tt
   ]
   hidden_effect = {
      if = {
         limit = {
            always = yes
            [[pirate] always = no ]
         }
         if = {
            limit = { 
               always = yes
               [[clear] always = no ]
            }
            spawn_rebels = {
               size = 1
               [[type] type = $type$ ]
               [[friend] friend = $friend$ ]
               [[religion] religion = $religion$ ]
               [[culture] culture = $culture$ ]
               [[leader] leader = $leader$ ]
               [[leader_dynasty] leader_dynasty = $leader_dynasty$ ]
               [[win] win = yes ]
               [[should_take_capital] should_take_capital = yes ]
               [[separatists_target] separatists_target = $separatists_target$ ]
               [[use_monarch_as_leader] use_monarch_as_leader = yes ]
               [[use_heir_as_leader] use_heir_as_leader = yes ]
               [[female] female = yes ]
            }
            set_variable = {
               which = rebel_size_stack
               value = $size$
            }
         }
         else = {
            set_variable = {
               which = rebel_size_stack
               value = 3
            }
         }
         set_variable = {
            which = rebels_in_province
            value = 600 #Base code always spawns rebels at this size
         }
         #Formula: f = forcelimit, d = development, s = stack size m = rebel size modifier
         #  round(3s+((f*d(s/2))/(f+d))*m)
         set_variable = {
            which = base_size
            value = 3
         }
         multiply_variable = {
            which = base_size
            which = rebel_size_stack
         }
         divide_variable = {
            which = rebel_size_stack
            value = 2
         }
         set_variable = {
            which = owner_forcelimit
            value = 0
         }
         set_variable = {
            which = province_dev
            value = 0
         }
         export_to_variable = {
            which = owner_forcelimit
            value = trigger_value:land_forcelimit
            who = owner
         }
         export_to_variable = {
            which = province_dev
            value = trigger_value:development
         }
         set_variable = {
            which = numerator
            which = owner_forcelimit
         }
         multiply_variable = {
            which = numerator
            which = province_dev
         }
         multiply_variable = {
            which = numerator
            which = rebel_size_stack
         }
         set_variable = {
            which = denominator
            which = owner_forcelimit
         }
         change_variable = {
            which = denominator
            which = province_dev
         }
         divide_variable = {
            which = numerator
            which = denominator
         }
         divide_variable = {
            which = numerator
            value = 2 # new unit size is doubled
         }
         set_variable = {
            which = size_mod
            value = 0
         }
         calculate_rebel_size_modifier = yes
         multiply_variable = {
            which = numerator
            which = rebel_size_modifier
         }
         change_variable = {
            which = numerator
            which = base_size
         }
         while = { #Cull rebels until it reaches the desired amount
            limit = {
               check_variable = {
                  which = rebels_in_province
                  which = numerator
               }
            }
            subtract_variable = {
               which = rebels_in_province
               value = 3
            }
            kill_units = {
               who = REB
               amount = 3
            }
         }
      }
      else = {
         set_variable = {
            which = pirate_size
            value = $size$
         }
         while = {
            limit = {
               check_variable = {
                  which = pirate_size
                  value = 1
               }
            }
            create_pirate = 1
            subtract_variable = {
               which = pirate_size
               value = 1
            }
         }
      }
   }
}
start_war_effect = { #Use this when generating wars for AI since they have limited situational CBs now. Also supports player wars
   if = {
      limit = {
         ai = yes
      }
      if = {
         limit = {
            $who$ = {
               ai = no
            }
         }
         if = {
            limit = {
               dip_tech = 23
            }
            declare_war_with_cb = {
               who = $who$
               casus_belli = cb_player_imperialism
            }
         }
         else = {
            declare_war_with_cb = {
               who = $who$
               casus_belli = cb_player_conquest
            }
         }
      }
      else = {
         if = {
            limit = {
               dip_tech = 23
            }
            declare_war_with_cb = {
               who = $who$
               casus_belli = cb_ai_imperialism
            }
         }
         else = {
            declare_war_with_cb = {
               who = $who$
               casus_belli = cb_ai_conquest
            }
         }
      }
   }
   else = {
      declare_war_with_cb = {
         who = $who$
         [[cb]
            casus_belli = $cb$
         ]
         [[war_goal]
            war_goal_province = $war_goal$
         ]
      }
   }
}
calculate_covert_action_cost = { #Calculates Covert action cost
   set_variable = {
      which = covert_action_cost
      value = 1
   }
   if = {
      limit = { has_idea = web_weaving }
      change_variable = {
         which = covert_action_cost
         value = -0.1
      }
   }
   if = {
      limit = { 
         has_active_policy = commercial_embassies
         NOT = { has_country_modifier = reverse_commercial_embassies }
      }
      change_variable = {
         which = covert_action_cost
         value = -0.33
      }
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         has_active_policy = ai_expansion_2
      }
      change_variable = {
         which = covert_action_cost
         value = -0.25
      }
   }
}
calculate_spy_cost = { #Calculates the Cost in Spy Network to subtract and displays the cost and effect in an event
   set_variable = {
      which = spy_network_base
      value = $base_cost$
   }  
   set_variable = {
      which = loop_limit
      which = spy_network_base
   }
   calculate_covert_action_cost = yes
   multiply_variable = {
   	which = spy_network_base
   	which = covert_action_cost #Modifies the cost of all covert actions (the ones i can modify...)
   }
   set_variable = {
      which = network_cost_tt
      which = spy_network_base
   }
   reverse_add_opinion = {
      who = $target_country$
      modifier =  action_$action$
   }
   reverse_add_opinion = {
      who = $target_country$
      modifier = temp_trigger_modifier
   }
   [[agitated_from]
      reverse_add_opinion = {
         who = FROM
         modifier = agitated_our_liberty
      }
      $target_country$ = {
         add_opinion = {
            who = FROM
            modifier = agitated_disloyal
         }
      }
   ]
   [[disrupted_from]
      reverse_add_opinion = {
         who = PREV
         modifier = action_$action$
      }
   ]
   set_country_flag = $action$_flag
   country_event = { id = cultural_events.85 } #$ACTION$ successful!
   $target_country$ = {
      set_country_flag = $action$_flag 
      country_event = { id = cultural_events.71 }  #$COUNTRY$ has performed $ACTION$ on us!
   }
   while = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = {
            which = spy_network_base
            value = 1
         }
         check_variable = {
            which = loop_limit
            value = 1
         }
      }
      subtract_variable = {
         which = spy_network_base
         value = 1
      }
      subtract_variable = {
         which = loop_limit
         value = 1
      }
      add_spy_network_in = {
         who = $target_country$
         value = -1
      }
      [[disrupted_from]
         add_spy_network_in = {
            who = PREV
            value = -1
         }
      ]
   }
}

add_merchants_slander_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = {
         has_country_modifier = slander_merchant2
      }
      add_country_modifier = {
         name = slander_merchant3
         duration = $duration$
      }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = {
         has_country_modifier = slander_merchant1
      }
      add_country_modifier = {
         name = slander_merchant2
         duration = $duration$
      }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = {
         has_country_modifier = slander_merchant0
      }
      add_country_modifier = {
         name = slander_merchant1
         duration = $duration$
      }
   }
   else = {
      add_country_modifier = {
         name = slander_merchant0
         duration = $duration$
      }
   }
}

#########################################################
#     POLICY MECHANIC (STATIC DONT REQUIRE CHANGING)

revoke_policy_effect = {
   hidden_effect = {
      if = {
         limit = {
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 1825 } #60 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 3650 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 1733 } #57 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 3466 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 1642 } #54 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 3284 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 1551 } #51 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 3102 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 1460 } #48 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 2920 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 1368 } #45 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 2736 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 1277 } #42 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 2554 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 1186 } #39 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 2372 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 1095 } #36 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 2190 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 1003 } #33 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 2006 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 912 } #30 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 1824 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 821 } #27 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 1622 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 730 } #24 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 1460 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 638 } #21 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 1276 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 547 } #18 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 1094 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 456 } #15 months
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 912 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            had_country_flag = { flag = $group$_cd_fl days = 1 } #Anywhere below 1.5 years
         }
         set_variable = { which = policy_time value = 730 }
      }
      [[adm]
         calculate_policy_cooldown = {
            policy = $policy$
            adm = yes
         }
      ]
      [[dip]
         calculate_policy_cooldown = {
            policy = $policy$
            dip = yes
         }
      ]
      [[mil]
         calculate_policy_cooldown = {
            policy = $policy$
            mil = yes
         }
      ]
      remove_country_modifier = reverse_$policy$
      clr_country_flag = $policy$_fl
      clr_country_flag = $group$_cd_fl
   }
}
calculate_policy_cooldown = {
   set_variable = {
      which = policy_cooldown_modifier
      value = 100
   }
   [[adm]
      export_to_variable = {
         which = category_modifier
         value = modifier:free_adm_policy
      }
   ]
   [[dip]
      export_to_variable = {
         which = category_modifier
         value = modifier:free_dip_policy
      }
   ]
   [[mil]
      export_to_variable = {
         which = category_modifier
         value = modifier:free_mil_policy
      }
   ]
   export_to_variable = {
      which = all_category_modifier
      value = modifier:free_policy
   }
   subtract_variable = {
      which = policy_cooldown_modifier
      which = all_category_modifier
   }
   subtract_variable = {
      which = policy_cooldown_modifier
      which = category_modifier
   }
   divide_variable = {
      which = policy_cooldown_modifier
      value = 100
   }
   multiply_variable = {
      which = policy_time
      which = policy_cooldown_modifier
   }
   set_country_flag = policyFL0
   while = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = {
            which = policy_time
            value = 30
         }
      }
      subtract_variable = {
         which = policy_time
         value = 30
      }
      apply_policy_cooldown = {
         policy = $policy$
      }
   }
   clr_policy_flags = yes
}
