add_reverse_policy_modifier = {
   add_country_modifier = {
      name = reverse_$policy$ #Add new reverse modifiers to common/mod_event_modifiers
      duration = -1
      desc = reverse_policy_desc
   }
}
clr_wt_modifiers = {
}
calc_war_taxes_cost = {
   set_variable = {
      which = war_taxes_mod
      value = 0
   }
   export_to_variable = {
      which = war_taxes_mod
      value = modifier:war_taxes_cost_modifier
   }
   divide_variable = {
      which = war_taxes_mod
      which = base_mobilisation_cost
   }
   set_variable = {
      which = est_loyalty_to_take
      value = 30 # Base loyalty to take
   }
   set_variable = {
      which = est_land_to_take
      value = 10 # Base crownland to take
   }
   set_variable = {
      which = est_mil_to_take
      value = 100 # Of each category
   }
   multiply_variable = {
      which = est_loyalty_to_take
      which = war_taxes_mod
   }
   multiply_variable = {
      which = est_land_to_take
      which = war_taxes_mod
   }
   multiply_variable = {
      which = est_mil_to_take
      which = war_taxes_mod
   }
   while = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = { which = est_mil_to_take value = 1 }
      }
      add_mil_power = -1
      add_adm_power = -1
      add_dip_power = -1
      subtract_variable = {
         which = est_mil_to_take
         value = 1
      }
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         NOT = { estate_loyalty = { estate = all loyalty = 20 } }
      }
      while = {
         limit = {
            check_variable = { which = est_land_to_take value = 0.5 }
         }
         change_estate_land_share = {
            estate = all
            share = 0.5
         }
         subtract_variable = {
            which = est_land_to_take
            value = 0.5
         }
      }
   }
   else = {
      while = {
         limit = {
            check_variable = { which = est_loyalty_to_take value = 1 }
         }
         add_estate_loyalty = {
            loyalty = -1
            estate = all
         }
         subtract_variable = {
            which = est_loyalty_to_take
            value = 1
         }
      }
   }
}
set_wt_cost_timer = {
   add_country_modifier = { name = wt_timer_1 duration = 365 }#hidden = yes }
   add_country_modifier = { name = wt_timer_2 duration = 730 }#hidden = yes }
   add_country_modifier = { name = wt_timer_3 duration = 1095 }#hidden = yes }
   add_country_modifier = { name = wt_timer_4 duration = 1460 }#hidden = yes }
   add_country_modifier = { name = wt_timer_5 duration = 1825 }#hidden = yes }
   add_country_modifier = { name = wt_timer_6 duration = 2190 }#hidden = yes }
   add_country_modifier = { name = wt_timer_7 duration = 2555 }#hidden = yes }
   add_country_modifier = { name = wt_timer_8 duration = 2920 }#hidden = yes }
   add_country_modifier = { name = wt_timer_9 duration = 3285 }#hidden = yes }
   add_country_modifier = { name = wt_timer_10 duration = 3650 }#hidden = yes }
}
set_mobilisation_level = { # Used for setting mobilisation to a specific level
   set_variable = {
      which = wartax_lvl
      value = $value$
   }
   hidden_effect = {
      clr_wt_modifiers = yes
      add_country_modifier = {
         name = wt_modifier_$value$
         duration = -1
      }
   }
}
set_mobilisation_tooltips = {
   set_variable = {
      which = mobilisation_tooltip_variable
      which = wartax_lvl
   }
   subtract_variable = {
      which = mobilisation_tooltip_variable
      value = 3
   }
   set_variable = {
      which = demobilisation_tooltip_variable
      which = mobilisation_tooltip_variable
   }
   multiply_variable = {
      which = demobilisation_tooltip_variable
      value = -1
   }
   export_to_variable = {
      which = mobilisation_cost_tooltip_var
      value = modifier:war_taxes_cost_modifier
   }
   subtract_variable = {
      which = mobilisation_cost_tooltip_var
      value = 1
   }
   multiply_variable = {
      which = mobilisation_cost_tooltip_var
      value = 100
   }
}
change_mobilisation_level = {
   [[cost]
      hidden_effect = {
         if = {
            limit = { ai = no }
            set_variable = {
               which = base_mobilisation_cost
               value = $cost$
            }
            calc_war_taxes_cost = yes
            set_wt_cost_timer = yes
         }
      }
   ]
   change_variable = {
      which = wartax_lvl
      value = $value$
   }
   hidden_effect = {
      clr_wt_modifiers = yes
      if = {
         limit = {
            is_mobilisation_level = { value = 6 }
         }
         add_country_modifier = { name = wt_modifier_6 duration = -1 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = {
            is_mobilisation_level = { value = 5 }
         }
         add_country_modifier = { name = wt_modifier_5 duration = -1 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            is_mobilisation_level = { value = 4 }
         }
         if = {
            limit = { ai = no }
            add_country_modifier = { name = wt_modifier_4 duration = -1 }
         }
         else = {
            add_country_modifier = { name = ai_mobilisation_modifier duration = -1 }
         }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = {
            is_mobilisation_level = { value = 3 }
         }
         add_country_modifier = { name = wt_modifier_3 duration = -1 hidden = yes }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            is_mobilisation_level = { value = 2 }
         }
         add_country_modifier = { name = wt_modifier_2 duration = -1 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            is_mobilisation_level = { value = 1 }
         }
         add_country_modifier = { name = wt_modifier_1 duration = -1 }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = { 
            is_mobilisation_level = { value = 0 }
         }
         add_country_modifier = { name = wt_modifier_0 duration = -1 }
      }
   }
}
start_incident_effect = {
   set_country_flag = active_incident_flag
   [[neo_confucianism]
      set_variable = { which = neo_confucianism_var value = 0 }
      country_event = { id = shinto_events.19 }
   ]
   [[nanban]
      set_variable = { which = nanban_var value = 4 }
      country_event = { id = shinto_events.25 }
   ]
   [[firearms]
      set_variable = { which = firearms_var value = 1 }
      country_event = { id = shinto_events.32 }
   ]
   [[christian]
      set_variable = { which = christian_var value = 0 }
      country_event = { id = shinto_events.38 }
   ]
   [[shogunate]
      set_variable = { which = shogunate_var value = 0 }
      country_event = { id = shinto_events.50 }
   ]
   [[ikko_ikki]
      set_variable = { which = ikko_ikki_var value = 0 }
      country_event = { id = shinto_events.13 }
   ]
   [[wokou]
      set_variable = { which = wokou_var value = 0 }
      country_event = { id = shinto_events.1 }
   ]
   [[urbanization]
      set_variable = { which = urbanization_var value = 0 }
      country_event = { id = shinto_events.7 }
   ]
}
end_incident_effect = {
   set_country_flag = shinto_incident_recent
   clr_country_flag = active_incident_flag
   add_isolationism = $isolationism$
   [[wokou]
      end_incident = incident_wokou
      set_variable = { which = wokou_var value = 0 }
      clr_country_flag = end_of_wokou_chain
   ]
   [[urbanization]
      end_incident = incident_urbanization
      set_variable = { which = urbanization_var value = 0 }
      clr_country_flag = end_of_urbanisation_chain
   ]
   [[ikko_ikki]
      end_incident = incident_ikko_shu
      set_variable = { which = ikko_ikki_var value = 0 }
      clr_country_flag = end_of_ikko_chain
   ]
   [[neo_confucianism]
      end_incident = incident_neo_confucianism
      set_variable = { which = neo_confucianism_var value = 0 }
      clr_country_flag = end_of_neo_confucianism_chain
   ]
   [[nanban]
      end_incident = incident_nanban
      set_variable = { which = nanban_var value = 0 }
      clr_country_flag = end_of_nanban_chain
   ]
   [[firearms]
      end_incident = incident_firearms
      set_variable = { which = firearms_var value = 0 }
      clr_country_flag = end_of_incident_firearms_chain
   ]
   [[christian]
      end_incident = incident_spread_of_christianity
      set_variable = { which = christian_var value = 0 }
      clr_country_flag = end_of_incident_spread_of_christianity_chain
   ]
   [[shogunate]
      end_incident = incident_shogunate_authority
      set_variable = { which = shogunate_var value = 0 }
      clr_country_flag = end_of_incident_shogunate_authority_chain
   ]
}
promote_officials_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			holy_order = promote_officials
		}
      owner = { calc_promote_officials_cost = yes }
		area = {
			limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
			set_promote_officials_modifier = yes
		}
		holy_order = reset_order
	}
}
set_promote_officials_modifier = {
   trigger_switch = {
      on_trigger = has_province_modifier
      officials1 = { remove_province_modifier = officials1 add_province_modifier = { name = officials2 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
      officials2 = { remove_province_modifier = officials2 add_province_modifier = { name = officials3 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
      officials3 = { remove_province_modifier = officials3 add_province_modifier = { name = officials4 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
      officials4 = { remove_province_modifier = officials4 add_province_modifier = { name = officials5 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
   }
   if = {
      limit = { NOT = { has_promote_officials_modifier = yes } }
      add_province_modifier = { name = officials1 duration = -1 hidden = yes }
   }
}
consecrate_metropolitan_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = {
         holy_order = consecrate_metropolitan_order
      }
      area = {
         limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
         #Gain scaled Patriach Authority based on development
         export_to_variable = {
            which = pa_to_add
            value = trigger_value:development
         }
         export_to_variable = {
            which = owner_dev
            value = trigger_value:total_development
            who = ROOT
         }
         divide_variable = {
            which = pa_to_add
            which = owner_dev
         }
         multiply_variable = {
            which = pa_to_add
            value = 100
         }
         #Capped at 3 per province
         if = {
            limit = {
               check_variable = {
                  which = pa_to_add
                  value = 3
               }
            }
            set_variable = {
               which = pa_to_add
               value = 3
            }
         }
         while = {
            limit = {
               check_variable = {
                  which = pa_to_add
                  value = 0.5
               }
            }
            subtract_variable = {
               which = pa_to_add
               value = 0.5
            }
            owner = { add_patriarch_authority = 0.005 }
         }
      }
   }
}
set_naval_supremacy_for = {
   every_country = {
      limit = {
         fighting_war_with = {
            who = $allies_of$
            enemy = $against_allies_of$
         }
      }
      every_country = {
         limit = {
            fighting_war_with = {
               who = $against_allies_of$
               enemy = $allies_of$
            }
         }
         remove_mutual_opinion_modifier_effect = {
            scope_country = PREV
            opinion_modifier = naval_supremacy_trigger
         }
         reverse_add_opinion = {
            who = PREV
            modifier = naval_supremacy_trigger
         }
      }
   }
}
recalculate_naval_supremacy = {
   unit_owner = {
      add_country_modifier = { name = naval_supremacy_recalc duration = 2 hidden = yes }
      save_event_target_as = winner 
   }
   enemy_unit = { 
      unit_owner = { save_event_target_as = loser } 
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         location = {
            light_ships_in_province = event_target:loser
         }
      }
      event_target:winner = {
         country_event = {
            id = cultural_events.61
            days = 1
         }
      }
   }
}
calc_naval_diceroll_effect = {
   random_list = {
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = dice_roll
            value = 1
         }
      }
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = dice_roll
            value = 1.25
         }
      }
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = dice_roll
            value = 1.5
         }
      }
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = dice_roll
            value = 1.75
         }
      }
      1 = {
         set_variable = {
            which = dice_roll
            value = 2
         }
      }
   }
   save_event_target_as = fort_prov
   random_neighbor_province = {
      limit = {
         fort_level = 1
         controller = { ROOT = { controlled_by = PREV } }
      }
      save_event_target_as = fort_prov
   }
   set_variable = {
      which = siege_tick
      which = enemy_siege_ability
   }
   change_variable = {
      which = siege_tick
      value = 1
   }
   export_to_variable = {
      which = fort_level
      value = trigger_value:fort_level
      who = event_target:fort_prov
   }
   multiply_variable = {
      which = fort_level
      value = 1.5
   }
   change_variable = {
      which = fort_level
      value = 1
   }
   divide_variable = {
      which = siege_tick
      which = fort_level
   }
   multiply_variable = {
      which = siege_tick
      which = dice_roll
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         NOT = {
            check_variable = {
               which = siege_progress
               value = 0
            }
         }
      }
      set_variable = {
         which = siege_progress
         value = 0
      }
   }
   change_variable = {
      which = siege_progress
      which = dice_roll
   }
   export_to_variable = {
	  which = true_fort_lvl
	  value = trigger_value:fort_level
	  who = event_target:fort_prov
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = {
            which = siege_progress
            which = true_fort_lvl
         }
      }
      event_target:fort_prov = {
         apply_naval_siege_effect = { who = $who$ }
      }
   }
}
add_naval_siege_tick_from = {
   calc_naval_diceroll_effect = {
      who = $who$
   }
   every_neighbor_province = {
      limit = {
         is_blockaded_by = $who$
         controller = { ROOT = { controlled_by = PREV } }
      }
      calc_naval_diceroll_effect = {
         who = $who$
      }
   }
}
apply_naval_siege_effect = {
   clr_province_flag = blockade_started
   set_variable = {
      which = siege_progress
      value = 0
   }
   set_variable = {
      which = enemy_siege_ability
      value = 0
   }
   remove_loot = {
      who = $who$
      amount = 100
   }
   change_controller = $who$
   if = {
      limit = {
         NOT = { has_terrain = teleporter }
      }
      add_province_modifier = {
         name = recently_naval_sieged
         duration = 365
         desc = naval_sieged_desc
      }
   }
}
find_invasion_target_province = {
   #Very bad case
   random_owned_province = {
      limit = {
         has_siege = no
         unit_in_battle = no
         is_island = no
         region_for_scope_province = {
            is_capital_of = event_target:country_to_go
         }
         OR = {
            NOT = { controlled_by = PREV }
            NOT = { fort_level = 1 }
         }
         NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = PREV } }
      }
      save_event_target_as = invasion_province
   }
   #Worst case scenario
   random_owned_province = {
      limit = {
         has_port = yes
         has_siege = no
         unit_in_battle = no
         is_island = no
         region_for_scope_province = {
            is_capital_of = event_target:country_to_go
         }
         OR = {
            NOT = { controlled_by = PREV }
            NOT = { fort_level = 1 }
         }
         NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = PREV } }
      }
      save_event_target_as = invasion_province
   }
   #Better case but still not ideal
   random_owned_province = {
      limit = {
         has_port = yes
         has_siege = no
         unit_in_battle = no
         is_island = no
         region_for_scope_province = {
            is_capital_of = event_target:country_to_go
         }
         OR = {
            NOT = { controlled_by = PREV }
            NOT = { fort_level = 1 }
         }
         NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = PREV } }

         all_neighbor_province = {
            NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = event_target:country_to_go } }
            all_neighbor_province = {
               NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = event_target:country_to_go } }
            }
         }
      }
      save_event_target_as = invasion_province
   }
   #Relatively Ideal case
   random_owned_province = {
      limit = {
         has_port = yes
         has_siege = no
         unit_in_battle = no
         is_island = no
         region_for_scope_province = {
            is_capital_of = event_target:country_to_go
         }
         OR = {
            NOT = { controlled_by = PREV }
            NOT = { fort_level = 1 }
         }
         NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = PREV } }

         all_neighbor_province = {
            NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = event_target:country_to_go } }
            all_neighbor_province = {
               NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = event_target:country_to_go } }
            }
         }

         any_neighbor_province = {
            land_units_in_province = { who = ROOT }
         }
      }
      save_event_target_as = invasion_province
   }
   #Good/Ideal case
   random_owned_province = {
      limit = {
         has_port = yes
         has_siege = no
         unit_in_battle = no
         is_island = no
         region_for_scope_province = {
            is_capital_of = event_target:country_to_go
         }
         OR = {
            NOT = { controlled_by = PREV }
            NOT = { fort_level = 1 }
         }
         NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = PREV } }

         all_neighbor_province = {
            NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = event_target:country_to_go } }
            all_neighbor_province = {
               NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = event_target:country_to_go } }
            }
         }

         land_units_in_province = { who = ROOT }
      }
      save_event_target_as = invasion_province
   }
   #Great case
   random_owned_province = {
      limit = {
         has_port = yes
         has_siege = no
         unit_in_battle = no
         is_island = no
         region_for_scope_province = {
            is_capital_of = event_target:country_to_go
         }
         OR = {
            NOT = { controlled_by = PREV }
            NOT = { fort_level = 1 }
         }
         NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = PREV } }

         all_neighbor_province = {
            NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = event_target:country_to_go } }
            all_neighbor_province = {
               NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = event_target:country_to_go } }
               all_neighbor_province = {
                  NOT = { land_units_in_province = { who = event_target:country_to_go } }
               }
            }
         }
         area_for_scope_province = {
            land_units_in_province = { who = ROOT }
         }
         defensive_terrain_trigger = yes
      }
      save_event_target_as = invasion_province
   }
}
teleport_units = {
   $target_province$ = { change_controller = ROOT }
   count_units_of_type = {
      type = infantry
      who = $unit_owner$
   }
   count_units_of_type = {
      type = cavalry
      who = $unit_owner$
   }
   count_units_of_type = {
      type = artillery
      who = $unit_owner$
   }
	while = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = infantry_count
				value = 1
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = infantry_count
			value = 5
		}
      $target_province$ = {
         spawn_infantry_effect = {
            who = $unit_owner$
         }
      }
	}
	while = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = cavalry_count
				value = 1
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = cavalry_count
			value = 5
		}
      $target_province$ = {
         spawn_cavalry_effect = {
            who = $unit_owner$
         }
      }
	}
	while = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = artillery_count
				value = 1
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = artillery_count
			value = 5
		}
      $target_province$ = {
         spawn_artillery_effect = {
            who = $unit_owner$
         }
      }
	}
}
new_coastal_raiding_effect = {
   #Raiding Coasts now gives monarch points
   #Formula is based off:

   #power_gained = ((dev-2)*0.1)+1)*5*(1+privateer_efficiency)

   #for each category
   if = {
      limit = {
         has_idea = naval_fighting_instruction #Naval Ideas
      }
      FROM = {
         every_neighbor_province = {
            limit = {
               has_province_modifier = slaves_raided
               NOT = { has_province_modifier = slaves_raided_trigger }
               owner = { 
                  has_opinion_modifier = {
                     who = ROOT
                     modifier = slaves_raided
                  }
               }
            }
            add_province_modifier = {
               name = slaves_raided_trigger
               duration = 3650
               hidden = yes
            }
            calc_dev_lost = { which = tax }
            calc_dev_lost = { which = production }
            calc_dev_lost = { which = manpower }
         }
      }
   }
}
calc_dev_lost = {
   export_to_variable = {
      which = $which$_dev
      value = trigger_value:base_$which$
   }
   subtract_variable = {
      which = $which$_dev
      value = 2
   }
   multiply_variable = {
      which = $which$_dev
      value = 0.1
   }
   change_variable = {
      which = $which$_dev
      value = 1
   }
   set_variable = {
      which = $which$_dup
      which = $which$_dev
   }
   while = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = {
            which = $which$_dev
            value = 1
         }
      }
      subtract_variable = {
         which = $which$_dev
         value = 1
      }
      add_base_$which$ = -1
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = {
            which = $which$_dup
            value = 1
         }
      }
      multiply_variable = {
         which = $which$_dup
         value = 5
      }
      export_to_variable = {
         which = privateer_efficiency
         value = modifier:privateer_efficiency
         who = ROOT
      }
      change_variable = {
         which = privateer_efficiency
         value = 1
      }
      multiply_variable = {
         which = $which$_dup
         which = privateer_efficiency
      }
      while = {
         limit = {
            check_variable = {
               which = $which$_dup
               value = 1
            }
         }
         subtract_variable = {
            which = $which$_dup
            value = 1
         }
         raid_coast_for = {
            who = ROOT
            $which$ = yes
         }
      }
   }
}
raid_coast_for = {
   [[tax]
      $who$ = { add_adm_power = 1 }
   ]
   [[production]
      $who$ = { add_dip_power = 1 }
   ]
   [[manpower]
      $who$ = { add_mil_power = 1 }
   ]
}

ajam_accept_ultimatum_effect = {
   exile_ruler_as = { name = muhammad_bin_baysonqor }
   define_ruler = {
      change_adm = -3
      change_mil = -3
      change_dip = -3
      dynasty = "Timurid"
      culture = uzbehk
   }
   if = {
      limit = { has_heir = yes }
      kill_heir = {}
   }
   azerbaijan_area = {
      limit = {
         owned_by = QOM
      }
      remove_core = QOM
      add_core = TAB
      cede_province = TAB
   }
   if = {
      limit = { overlord_of = ARD }
      add_truce_with = ARD
      ARD = { grant_independence = yes }
   }
   every_country = {
      limit = {
         OR = {
            tag = TIM
            is_subject_of = TIM
         }
      }
      ROOT = { add_truce_with = PREV }
   }
   add_prestige = -50
   add_legitimacy_equivalent = { amount = -25 }
   add_adm_power = -100
   add_dip_power = -100
   add_mil_power = -100
   add_stability = -1
}

      add_stability = -1
   }
}

   }
}
timurid_prince_conquest_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = {
         FROM = { dynasty = "Timurid" }
         owner = { 
            dynasty = "Timurid" 
            OR = {
               has_reform = timurid_prince
               tag = TIM
            }
         }
      }
      add_core = owner
   }
}
add_ruler_skill_or_mil_power = {
   #This maximizes the benefit of effects that change monarch skill
   if = {
      limit = {
         NOT = { mil = 6 }
      }
      change_mil = 1
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = {
         has_heir = yes
         NOT = { heir_mil = 6 }
      }
      change_heir_mil = 1
   }
   else = {
      add_mil_power = 200
   }
}
add_ruler_skill_or_adm_power = {
   #This maximizes the benefit of effects that change monarch skill
   if = {
      limit = {
         NOT = { adm = 6 }
      }
      change_adm = 1
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = {
         has_heir = yes
         NOT = { heir_adm = 6 }
      }
      change_heir_adm = 1
   }
   else = {
      add_adm_power = 200
   }
}

abdal_latif_succession_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = abdal_latif_succession_happened } }
      #If Abdal-Latif dies in Balkh he will also die in Transoxiana
      if = {
         limit = {
            has_ruler_flag = abdal_latif_timurid
            TRS = { has_heir_flag = abdal_latif_timurid }
         }
         set_global_flag = abdal_latif_succession_happened
         TRS = { kill_heir = {} }
      }
      #If Abdal-Latif dies in Transoxiana he will also die in Balkh
      if = {
         limit = {
            has_heir_flag = abdal_latif_timurid
            ISF = { has_ruler_flag = abdal_latif_timurid }
         }
         set_global_flag = abdal_latif_succession_happened
         ISF = { kill_ruler = yes }
      }
   }
}
sufi_autonomy_privilege_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = { 
         NOT = { religion = owner }
         owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_tim_sufi_autonomy }
      }
      add_province_modifier = {
         name = sufi_autonomy_modifier
         duration = -1
      }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = {
         has_province_modifier = sufi_autonomy_modifier
         religion = owner
      }
      remove_province_modifier = sufi_autonomy_modifier
   }
}
#1.34 -> Fixing some trashy code
add_noble_loyalty_from_fort_built = {
   FROM  = {
      if  = {
         limit = { has_government_attribute = on_fort_built_nobles_loyalty }
         trigger_switch = {
            on_trigger = has_building
            fort_15th = {
               if = {
                  limit = { NOT = { can_build = fort_16th } }
                  add_estate_loyalty_by_class_mil = {
                     loyalty = 2
                  }
               }
            }
            fort_16th = {
               if = {
                  limit = { NOT = { can_build = fort_17th } }
                  add_estate_loyalty_by_class_mil = {
                     loyalty = 2
                  }
               }
            }
            fort_17th = {
               if = {
                  limit = { NOT = { can_build = fort_18th } }
                  add_estate_loyalty_by_class_mil = {
                     loyalty = 2
                  }
               }
            }
            fort_18th = {
               add_estate_loyalty_by_class_mil = {
                  loyalty = 2
               }
            }
         }
         if = {
            limit = { NOT = { has_fort_building_trigger = yes } }
            add_estate_loyalty_by_class_mil = {
               loyalty = -2
            }
         }
      }
   }
}

count_units_of_type = {
   export_to_variable = {
      which = $type$_count
      value = trigger_value:$type$_in_province
   }
   kill_units = {
      who = $who$
      type = $type$
   }
   export_to_variable = {
      which = $type$
      value = trigger_value:$type$_in_province
   }
   subtract_variable = {
      which = $type$_count
      which = $type$
   }
}
replace_units = {
	while = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = $who$_$type$_count
				value = 1
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = $who$_$type$_count
			value = 5
		}
      $target_province$ = {
         spawn_$type$_effect = {
            who = $who$
         }
      }
	}
}
spawn_infantry_effect = {
   infantry = $who$
   infantry = $who$
   infantry = $who$
   infantry = $who$
   infantry = $who$
}
spawn_cavalry_effect = {
	cavalry = $who$
   cavalry = $who$
   cavalry = $who$
   cavalry = $who$
   cavalry = $who$
}
spawn_artillery_effect = {
   artillery = $who$
   artillery = $who$
   artillery = $who$
   artillery = $who$
   artillery = $who$
}
on_new_age_mercenary_cost_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = { 
         current_age = age_of_reformation 
      }
      add_country_modifier = {
         name = mercs_reformation
         duration = -1
         hidden = yes
      }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = { 
         current_age = age_of_absolutism 
      }
      remove_country_modifier = mercs_reformation
      add_country_modifier  = {
         name = mercs_absolutism
         duration = -1
         hidden = yes
      }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = { current_age = age_of_industry }
      remove_country_modifier = mercs_absolutism
      add_country_modifier = {
         name = mercs_revolutions
         duration = -1
         hidden = yes
      }
   }
}

   remove_country_modifier = merc_disc8
   remove_country_modifier = merc_disc10
   remove_country_modifier = merc_disc12
   remove_country_modifier = merc_disc14
   remove_country_modifier = merc_disc16
   remove_country_modifier = merc_disc18
   remove_country_modifier = merc_disc20

   }
}
apply_merc_discipline_effect = {
   trigger_switch = {
      on_trigger = has_country_modifier
      merc_disc0 = { reset_modifier = { which = merc_disc0 new_modifier = merc_disc2 scope = country } }
      merc_disc2 = { reset_modifier = { which = merc_disc2 new_modifier = merc_disc4 scope = country } }
      merc_disc4 = { reset_modifier = { which = merc_disc4 new_modifier = merc_disc6 scope = country } }
      merc_disc6 = { reset_modifier = { which = merc_disc6 new_modifier = merc_disc8 scope = country } }
      merc_disc8 = { reset_modifier = { which = merc_disc8 new_modifier = merc_disc10 scope = country } }
      merc_disc10 = { reset_modifier = { which = merc_disc10 new_modifier = merc_disc12 scope = country } }
      merc_disc12 = { reset_modifier = { which = merc_disc12 new_modifier = merc_disc14 scope = country } }
      merc_disc14 = { reset_modifier = { which = merc_disc14 new_modifier = merc_disc16 scope = country } }
      merc_disc16 = { reset_modifier = { which = merc_disc16 new_modifier = merc_disc18 scope = country } }
      merc_disc18 = { reset_modifier = { which = merc_disc18 new_modifier = merc_disc20 scope = country } }
   }
}
on_siege_won_teleporter_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = { has_terrain = teleporter }
      controller = { save_event_target_as = teleporter_controller }
      every_neighbor_province = {
         limit = { 
            is_empty = no
            owner = { war_with = event_target:teleporter_controller } 
         }
         add_province_modifier = {
            name = local_teleporter_captured
            duration = 180
         }
         change_controller = event_target:teleporter_controller
      }
   }
}
on_conquistador_teleporter_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = {
         FROM = { ai = no } #AI won't exploit this
         has_province_modifier = teleporter_province_modifier
      }
      if = {
         limit = {
            OR = {
               any_neighbor_province = {
                  NOT = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = FROM }
               }
               all_empty_neighbor_province = {
                  NOT = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = FROM }
               }
            }
         }
         undiscover_country = FROM #Can only use teleporters if one side is owned & otherside is uncolonized OR both sides are owned
      }
   }
}

         estate = estate_$estate$
         influence = 5
         duration = 7300
         short = yes
         desc = EST_VAL_DIET_SUMMONED
      }
   }
}

         investor = $who$
         investment = $which$
      }
   }
}
allow_privilege_revoke_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = {
            which = estate_revoke_var
            value = 1
         }
      }
      custom_tooltip = privilege_can_be_revoked_tooltip
      hidden_effect = {
         random_owned_province = { 
            limit = {
               island = no
               if = {
                  limit = { owner = { ai = yes } }
                  same_continent = capital
               }
            }  
            start_revolt = {
               size = 2
            }
         }
         random_owned_province = { 
            limit = {
               island = no
               if = {
                  limit = { owner = { ai = yes } }
                  same_continent = capital
               }
            } 
            start_revolt = {
               size = 1
            }
         }
         random_owned_province = { 
            limit = {
               island = no
               if = {
                  limit = { owner = { ai = yes } }
                  same_continent = capital
               }
            } 
            start_revolt = {
               size = 1
            }
         }
         add_stability = -1
         set_variable = {
            which = estate_revoke_var
            value = 0
         }
         random_estate = {
            add_influence = -5
            desc = CAC_can_revoke_privilege_influence_modifier
            duration = 1095
         }
      }
   }
   #Generic stuff thats added regardless, try to add stuff for religion/region based stuff for flavour
   add_piety = 0.05
   add_mandate = 5
   add_karma = 5
   add_church_power = 5
   add_fervor = 5
   add_papal_influence = 5
   add_doom = -5
   add_authority = 5
   if = {
      limit = { 
         religion_group = pagan 
         NOT = { government = tribal }
      }
      random_owned_province = {
         limit = {
            NOT = { current_institution = 50 }
         }
         area = {
            limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
            add_next_institution_embracement = 10
         }
      }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = {
         government = tribal
      }
      add_country_modifier = {
         name = tribes_resisting_cac
         duration = 730
      }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = { religion = shinto }
      add_legitimacy_equivalent = { amount = 5 }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = { religion = hinduism }
      add_estate_influence_modifier = {
         estate = estate_brahmins
         influence = -5
         duration = 365
         desc = cac_declining_castes
      }
      add_estate_influence_modifier = {
         estate = estate_jains
         influence = -5
         duration = 365
         desc = cac_declining_castes
      }
      add_estate_influence_modifier = {
         estate = estate_vaisyas
         influence = -5
         duration = 365
         desc = cac_declining_castes
      }
   }
}
disable_privilege_revoke_effect = {
   if = {

         check_variable = {
            which = estate_revoke_var

         }

   random_estate = {
      add_loyalty = 10
   }
   add_estate_loyalty = {
      estate = all
      loyalty = 5
   }
   add_piety = -0.05
   add_mandate = -5
   add_karma = -5
   add_doom = 5
   add_authority = -5
   if = {
      limit = { 
         religion_group = pagan 
         NOT = { government = tribal }
      }
      add_country_modifier = {
         name = cac_pagan_declining_state_influence
         duration = 730
      }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = {
         religion_group = christian
      }
      add_country_modifier = {
         name = cac_factional_influence
         duration = 730
      }
   }
   else_if = {

         government = tribal
      }
      random_owned_province = {
         limit = { unrest = 1 }

            add_unrest = -5
         }
      }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = {
         religion_group = eastern
      }

         name = cac_eastern_advisors
         duration = 730
      }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = { religion = hinduism }
      add_estate_influence_modifier = {
         estate = estate_brahmins
         influence = 5
         duration = 365
         desc = cac_strong_castes
      }
      add_estate_influence_modifier = {
         estate = estate_jains
         influence = 5
         duration = 365
         desc = cac_strong_castes
      }
      add_estate_influence_modifier = {
         estate = estate_vaisyas
         influence = 5
         duration = 365
         desc = cac_strong_castes
      }
   }
}
diceroll_bonus_in_gaelic_land_effect = { # This might tank performance! Don't call this effect unless the cultural centre is tier 2+
   hidden_effect = {
      if = {
         limit = {
            area_for_scope_province = {
               controlled_by = event_target:gaelic_country
            }
            area_for_scope_province = {
               has_fort_building_trigger = yes
               OR = {
                  has_terrain = mountain
                  has_terrain = highlands
                  has_terrain = hills
                  culture_group = gaelic
               }
            }
         }
         area = {
            limit = { 
               has_fort_building_trigger = yes 
               OR = {
                  has_terrain = mountain
                  has_terrain = highlands
                  has_terrain = hills
                  culture_group = gaelic
               }
               OR = {
                  controlled_by = event_target:gaelic_country
                  owner = { 
                     war_with = event_target:gaelic_country
                  }
               }
            }
            if = {
               limit = { 
                  controlled_by = event_target:gaelic_country 
               }
               add_gaelic_defender_diceroll_bonus = yes
            }
            else = {
               add_gaelic_attacker_diceroll_bonus = yes
            }
         }
      }
      else_if = {
         limit = {
            area_for_scope_province = {
               has_gaelic_diceroll_bonus = yes
            }
         }
         area = {
            limit = {
               OR = {
                  AND = {
                     NOT = { culture_group = gaelic }
                     NOT = { has_terrain = mountain }
                     NOT = { has_terrain = highlands }
                     NOT = { has_terrain = hills }
                  }
                  NOT = { has_fort_building_trigger = yes }
               }
               has_gaelic_diceroll_bonus = yes
            }
            remove_gaelic_diceroll_bonus = yes
         }
      }
   }
}
add_gaelic_defender_diceroll_bonus = {
   remove_gaelic_diceroll_bonus = yes
}
add_gaelic_attacker_diceroll_bonus = {
   remove_gaelic_diceroll_bonus = yes
}
remove_gaelic_diceroll_bonus = {
   remove_province_modifier = gaelic_defender_diceroll_2
   remove_province_modifier = gaelic_defender_diceroll_3
   remove_province_modifier = gaelic_attacker_diceroll_2
   remove_province_modifier = gaelic_attacker_diceroll_3
}
on_gaelic_war_won_effect = { # Just to absolutely make sure the bonuses are removed after the war ends
}
on_colonial_war_won_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = cant_call_allies_flag
				FROM = { has_country_flag = cant_call_allies_flag }
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = fighting_colonial_war
		clr_country_flag = cant_call_allies_flag
      remove_country_modifier = mediocre_colonial_benefits_modifier_country
      remove_country_modifier = colonial_benefits_modifier_country
      every_owned_province = {
         remove_province_modifier = colonial_benefits_modifier_province
         remove_province_modifier = mediocre_colonial_benefits_modifier_province
      }
		FROM = { 
			clr_country_flag = fighting_colonial_war 
			clr_country_flag = cant_call_allies_flag
         remove_country_modifier = mediocre_colonial_benefits_modifier_country
         remove_country_modifier = colonial_benefits_modifier_country
         every_owned_province = {
            remove_province_modifier = colonial_benefits_modifier_province
            remove_province_modifier = mediocre_colonial_benefits_modifier_province
         }
		}
	}
}
update_building_area_modifiers = { # This is for updating buildings that apply area modifiers, eg forts
   if = {
      limit = {
         area_for_scope_province = {
            OR = {
               has_building = state_house
               has_province_modifier = state_house_modifier
               has_province_modifier = state_house_modifier_boost
            }
            owner = { ROOT = { owned_by = PREV } }
         }
      }
      if = {
         limit = {
            OR = {
               trade_goods = glass
               trade_goods = paper
               trade_goods = gems
            }
         }
         add_province_modifier = {
            name = state_house_modifier_boost
            duration = -1
            hidden = yes
         }
         remove_province_modifier = state_house_modifier
      }
      else = {
         add_province_modifier = {
            name = state_house_modifier
            duration = -1
            hidden = yes
         }
         remove_province_modifier = state_house_modifier_boost
      }
   }
}
on_trade_good_changed_buildings_effect = { # Use this for changing buildings when the trade good changes
   if = {
      limit = {
         has_province_modifier = state_house_modifier_boost
         NOT = { trade_goods = glass }
         NOT = { trade_goods = gems }
         NOT = { trade_goods = paper }
      }
      remove_province_modifier = state_house_modifier_boost
      add_province_modifier = {
         name = state_house_modifier
         duration = -1
         hidden = yes
      }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = {
         OR = {
            trade_goods = glass
            trade_goods = gems
            trade_goods = paper
         }
         has_province_modifier = state_house_modifier
      }
      remove_province_modifier = state_house_modifier
      add_province_modifier = {
         name = state_house_modifier_boost
         duration = -1
         hidden = yes
      }
   }
}
on_war_won_forcelimit_effect = {
   remove_country_modifier = "ai_war_commit"
   remove_country_modifier = "ai_war_commit2"
   FROM = { remove_country_modifier = "ai_war_commit" }
   FROM = { remove_country_modifier = "ai_war_commit2" }
}
calc_war_tryhard_effect = {
   if = {
      limit = {
         is_at_war = yes
         ai = yes
         is_bankrupt = no
         NOT = { has_country_modifier = "ai_war_commit" }
		   OR = {
			   is_mobilisation_level = {
				   value = 4 # Commit harder if you've raised mobilisation
			   }
			   any_war_enemy_country = {
				   OR = {
					   is_mobilisation_level = {
						   value = 4 # Commit harder if enemies have raised mobilisation
					   }
					   AND = {
						   ai = no # Commit harder if the player is beating you
						   war_score_against = {
							   who = PREV
							   value = 25
						   }
					   }
					   AND = {
						   war_score_against = {
							   who = PREV # Commit harder if you're losing and enemy has commited harder
							   value = 25
						   }
						   army_size_percentage = 1.5
					   }
				   }
			   }
			   calc_true_if = {
				   amount = 2 # Commit harder if you're being ganked
				   all_war_enemy_countries = {
					   is_in_war = { attacker_leader = THIS defenders = PREV }
				   }
			   }
            has_country_flag = important_war
		   }
      }
      add_country_modifier = {
         name = "ai_war_commit"
         duration = -1
         hidden = yes
      }
   }
   else_if = {
      limit = {
         has_country_modifier = "ai_war_commit"
         NOT = { has_country_modifier = "ai_war_commit2" }
         any_war_enemy_country = {
            war_score_against = {
               who = PREV
               value = 50
            }
            NOT = {
               war_score_against = {
                  who = PREV
                  value = 80
               }
            }
         }
      }
      add_country_modifier = {
         name = "ai_war_commit2"
         duration = -1
         hidden = yes
      }
   }
}
province_owner_change_kyoto_effect = {
   # Root = kyoto
   # From = old owner
   # event_target:kyoto_owner = current owner
   if = {
      limit = {
         province_id = 1020 # Kyoto
      }
      owner = {
         save_event_target_as = kyoto_owner
         if = {
            limit = {
               is_subject = yes
            }
            overlord = {
               save_event_target_as = kyoto_overlord
            }
         }
      }
      event_target:kyoto_owner = {
         if = {
            limit = { is_subject = yes }
            ROOT = {
               cede_province = event_target:kyoto_overlord
            }
            event_target:kyoto_overlord = {
               set_country_flag = transfer_from_subject
            }
         }
         else = {
            set_country_flag = fall_of_kyoto_fl
         }
      }
   }
}
develop_provinces_in_terrain = {
   set_variable = {
      which = loop_fail
      value = 0
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         $power$_power = 950
      }
      while = {
         limit = {
            $power$_power = 200
            NOT = {
               check_variable = {
                  which = loop_fail
                  value = 1
               }
            }
         }
         random_owned_province = {
            limit = {
               [[farmlands]
                  OR = {
                     has_terrain = drylands
                     has_terrain = farmlands
                     has_terrain = grasslands
                  }
               ]
               [[mildly_bad]
                  OR = {
                     has_terrain = hills
                     has_terrain = woods
                     has_terrain = coastline
                     has_terrain = steppe
                     has_terrain = forest
                     has_terrain = savannah
                  }
               ]
               [[bad]
                  OR = {
                     has_terrain = highlands
                     has_terrain = marsh
                  }
               ]
               [[very_bad]
                  OR = {
                     has_terrain = jungle
                     has_terrain = mountain
                     has_terrain = glacier
                     has_terrain = desert
                     has_terrain = coastal_desert
                  }
               ]
               NOT = { development = $below_development$ }
            }
            export_to_variable = {
               which = local_dev_cost
               value = modifier:local_development_cost
            }
            export_to_variable = {
               which = local_dev_cost_modifier
               value = modifier:local_development_cost_modifier
            }
            change_variable = {
               which = local_dev_cost
               value = 1
            }
            change_variable = {
               which = local_dev_cost_modifier
               value = 1
            }
            set_variable = {
               which = dev_cost
               value = 50
            }
            multiply_variable = {
               which = dev_cost
               which = local_dev_cost_modifier
            }
            multiply_variable = {
               which = dev_cost
               which = local_dev_cost
            }
            ROOT = {
               subtract_variable = {
                  which = loop_fail
                  value = 1
               }
               while = {
                  limit = {
                     PREV = {
                        check_variable = {
                           which = dev_cost
                           value = 1
                        }
                     }
                  }
                  PREV = {
                     subtract_variable = {
                        which = dev_cost
                        value = 10
                     }
                  }
                  add_$power$_power = -10
               }
            }
            add_base_$type$ = 1
         }
         change_variable = {
            which = loop_fail
            value = 1
         }
      }
   }
}
change_random_province_to_silk_in_persia = {
	random_owned_province = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { trade_goods = silk }
			OR = {
				region = khorasan_region
				region = persia_region
			}
			owned_by = ROOT
			NOT = {
				area_for_scope_province = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = silk
						development = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					OR = {
						trade_goods = silk
						development = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			development = 10
		}
		change_trade_goods = silk
	}
}

remove_cores = { # used in history files to wipe cores from a province
   every_core_country = {
      remove_core = PREV
   }
}

#  Add new mechanics here

#Use this within loops to reapply dynamic modifiers
reset_modifier = {
   remove_$scope$_modifier = $which$
   add_$scope$_modifier = { name = $new_modifier$ duration = -1 hidden = yes }
   [[power]
      remove_trade_modifier = {
         key = "Slandered Merchants "
         who = ROOT
      }
      add_trade_modifier = {
         who = ROOT
         key = "Slandered Merchants "
         power = $power$
         duration = 1825
      }
   ]
}

calc_promote_officials_cost = {
   set_variable = {
      which = promote_officials_cost_modifier
      value = 2
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         has_idea = administrative_efficiency_idea
      }
      multiply_variable = {
         which = promote_officials_cost_modifier
         value = 0.5
      }
   }
   while = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = {
            which = promote_officials_cost_modifier
            value = 0.05
         }
      }
      subtract_variable = {
         which = promote_officials_cost_modifier
         value = 0.05
      }
      add_corruption = 0.05
   }
}

calc_harmony_lost_on_conversion = {
   hidden_effect = {
      if = {
         limit = {
            owner = {
               has_harmony = yes
            }
         }
         set_variable = {
            which = harmony_refund_modifier
            value = 0
         }
         export_to_variable = {
            which = base_harmony_loss
            value = trigger_value:development
         }
         divide_variable = {
            which = base_harmony_loss
            value = 2
         }
         if = {
            limit = {
               has_province_modifier = eoc_converting_miao_modifier # 50% refund
            }
            change_variable = {
               which = harmony_refund_modifier
               value = 0.5
            }
         }
         if = {
            limit = {
               owner = { has_idea = inquisition } # 75% refund
            }
            change_variable = {
               which = harmony_refund_modifier
               value = 0.75
            }
         }
         if = {
            limit = {
               check_variable = {
                  which = harmony_refund_modifier
                  value = 1
               }
            }
            set_variable = {
               which = harmony_refund_modifier
               value = 1
            }
         }
         multiply_variable = {
            which = base_harmony_loss
            which = harmony_refund_modifier
         }
         while = {
            limit = {
               check_variable = {
                  which = base_harmony_loss
                  value = 0.5
               }
            }
            subtract_variable = {
               which = base_harmony_loss
               value = 0.5
            }
            owner = {
               add_harmony = 0.5
            }
         }
      }
   }
}

on_battle_lost_army_drill_effect = { # Calculate army drill loss from losing a battle
   if = {
      limit = {
         FROM = {
            army_professionalism = 0.01
            is_free_or_tributary_trigger = yes
         }
         num_of_units_in_province = {
            who = FROM
            amount = 15
         }
         unit_has_leader = yes
         is_sea = no
         NOT = { has_province_modifier = "recently_lost_battle_timer" } # so after battles dont count
      }
      add_province_modifier = {
         name = "recently_lost_battle_timer"
         duration = 30
         hidden = yes
      }
      FROM = {
         set_variable = {
            which = base_drill_loss
            value = 1.5
         }
         if = {
            limit = { ai = yes }
            set_variable = {
               which = base_drill_loss
               value = 1
            } 
         }
         export_to_variable = {
            which = drill_decay_mod
            value = modifier:drill_decay_modifier
         }
         change_variable = {
            which = drill_decay_mod
            value = 1
         }
         multiply_variable = {
            which = base_drill_loss
            which = drill_decay_mod
         }
         while = {
            limit = {
               check_variable = {
                  which = base_drill_loss
                  value = 0.25
               }
            }
            subtract_variable = {
               which = base_drill_loss
               value = 0.25
            }
            add_army_professionalism = -0.0025
         }
      }
   }
}

on_war_lost_army_drill_effect = { # Calculate army drill loss from losing a war
   if = {
      limit = {
         army_professionalism = 0.01
      }
      set_variable = {
         which = base_drill_loss
         value = 10
      }
      export_to_variable = {
         which = drill_decay_mod
         value = modifier:drill_decay_modifier
      }
      multiply_variable = {
         which = base_drill_loss
         which = drill_decay_mod
      }
      while = {
         limit = {
            check_variable = {
               which = base_drill_loss
               value = 0.5
            }
         }
         subtract_variable = {
            which = base_drill_loss
            value = 0.5
         }
         add_army_professionalism = -0.005
      }
   }
}




# SPY NETWORK EFFECTS moved here to maintain readability across other files.

raid_coffers_effect = {
   #Do this first for tooltips
	if = {
		limit = {
			monthly_income = $target$
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = income_to_add
			value = 0
		}
		export_to_variable = {
			which = income_to_add
			value = trigger_value:monthly_income
			who = $target$
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = income_to_add
			value = 6
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			which = income_to_add
			value = 0
		}
		export_to_variable = {
			which = income_to_add
			value = trigger_value:monthly_income
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = income_to_add
			value = 6
		}
	}
	calculate_spy_cost = {
		base_cost = 50
		target_country = $target$
		action = raided_coffers
	}
	while = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = income_to_add
				value = 1
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = income_to_add
			value = 1
		}
		add_treasury = 1
		$target$ = { add_treasury = -1 }
   }
	$target$ = { add_inflation = 2 }
}

slander_merchants_effect = {
   calculate_spy_cost = {
      base_cost = 100
      target_country = $target$
      action = slandered_merchants
   }
   every_trade_node = {
      limit = {
         has_most_province_trade_power = $target$
      }
      random_trade_node_member_province = {
         limit = {
            owned_by = $target$
         }
         set_variable = {
            which = tp_var
            value = 0
         }
         every_trade_node_member_province = {
            limit = {
               owned_by = $target$
               NOT = { province_id = PREV }
            }
            export_to_variable = {
               which = tp_var
               value = trigger_value:province_trade_power
            }
            PREV = {
               change_variable = {
                  which = tp_var
                  which = PREV
               }
            }
         }
         add_province_modifier = {
            name = slander0
            duration = -1
            hidden = yes
         }
         while = {
            limit = {
               check_variable = {
                  which = tp_var
                  value = 1
               }
            }
            subtract_variable = {
               which = tp_var
               value = 20
            }
            apply_slander_merchants_effect = yes
         }
      }
   }
   $target$ = {
      add_casus_belli = {
         target = ROOT
         type = cb_slandered_merchants
         months = 60
      }
   }
   add_merchants_slander_effect = {
      duration = 1825
   }
}

bribe_recruits_effect = {
   #Do this first for tooltips:
   if = {
      limit = {
         variable_arithmetic_trigger = {
            export_to_variable = {
               which = our_max_manpower
               value = trigger_value:max_manpower
            }
            export_to_variable = {
               which = their_max_manpower
               value = trigger_value:max_manpower
               who = $target$
            }
            check_variable = {
               #If our Manpower Pool > Their Manpower Pool
               which = our_max_manpower
               which = their_max_manpower
            }
         }
      }
      set_variable = {
         which = manpower_to_take
         value = 0
      }
      export_to_variable = {
         which = manpower_to_take
         value = trigger_value:max_manpower
         who = $target$
      }
      export_to_variable = {
         which = mrs_value
         value = modifier:manpower_recovery_speed
         who = $target$
      }
      change_variable = {
         which = mrs_value
         value = 1
      }
      multiply_variable = {
         which = manpower_to_take
         value = 0.1
      }
      multiply_variable = {
         which = manpower_to_take
         which = mrs_value
      }
   }
   else = {
      set_variable = {
         which = manpower_to_take
         value = 0
      }
      export_to_variable = {
         which = manpower_to_take
         value = trigger_value:max_manpower
      }
      export_to_variable = {
         which = mrs_value
         value = modifier:manpower_recovery_speed
      }
      change_variable = {
         which = mrs_value
         value = 1
      }
      multiply_variable = {
         which = manpower_to_take
         value = 0.1
      }
      multiply_variable = {
         which = manpower_to_take
         which = mrs_value
      }
   }
   calculate_spy_cost = {
      base_cost = 70
      target_country = $target$
      action = bribed_recruits
   }
   while = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = {
            which = manpower_to_take
            value = 1
         }
      }
      subtract_variable = {
         which = manpower_to_take
         value = 1
      }
      add_manpower = 1
      $target$ = { add_manpower = -1 }
   }
}

corrupt_officials_effect = {
   #Do this first for tooltip:
   if = {
      #Generation better than FROM
      limit = {
         OR = {
            AND = {
               adm = $target$
               dip = $target$
            }
            AND = {
               adm = $target$
               mil = $target$
            }
            AND = {
               dip = $target$
               mil = $target$
            }
         }
      }
      set_variable = {
         which = from_adm
         value = 0
      }
      set_variable = {
         which = from_dip
         value = 0
      }
      set_variable = {
         which = from_mil
         value = 0
      }
      export_to_variable = {
         which = from_adm
         value = trigger_value:monthly_adm
         who = $target$
      }
      export_to_variable = {
         which = from_dip
         value = trigger_value:monthly_dip
         who = $target$
      }
      export_to_variable = {
         which = from_mil
         value = trigger_value:monthly_mil
         who = $target$
      }
      multiply_variable = {
         which = from_dip
         value = 4
      }
      multiply_variable = {
         which = from_adm
         value = 4
      }
      multiply_variable = {
         which = from_mil
         value = 4
      }
   }
   else = {
      set_variable = {
         which = from_adm
         value = 0
      }
      set_variable = {
         which = from_dip
         value = 0
      }
      set_variable = {
         which = from_mil
         value = 0
      }
      export_to_variable = {
         which = from_adm
         value = trigger_value:monthly_adm
      }
      export_to_variable = {
         which = from_dip
         value = trigger_value:monthly_dip
      }
      export_to_variable = {
         which = from_mil
         value = trigger_value:monthly_mil
      }
      multiply_variable = {
         which = from_dip
         value = 4
      }
      multiply_variable = {
         which = from_adm
         value = 4
      }
      multiply_variable = {
         which = from_mil
         value = 4
      }
   }
   calculate_spy_cost = {
      base_cost = 50
      target_country = $target$
      action = corrupted_officials
   }
   while = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = {
            which = from_adm
            value = 1
         }
      }
      subtract_variable = {
         which = from_adm
         value = 1
      }
      add_adm_power = 1
      $target$ = { add_adm_power = -1 }
   }
   while = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = {
            which = from_dip
            value = 1
         }
      }
      subtract_variable = {
         which = from_dip
         value = 1
      }
      add_dip_power = 1
      $target$ = { add_dip_power = -1 }
   }
   while = {
      limit = {
         check_variable = {
            which = from_mil
            value = 1
         }
      }
      subtract_variable = {
         which = from_mil
         value = 1
      }
      add_mil_power = 1
      $target$ = { add_mil_power = -1 }
   }
   $target$ = {
      add_corruption = 1
   }
   if = {
      limit = {
         ai = yes
      }
      add_corruption = -1 # THis is because the AI sucks at dealing with corruption, so corrupting someone else uncorrupts you?..
   }
}
